a	<h3>a</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>art.</i></font><br>表示“一(个, 件…)<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He needs an assistant.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他需要一位助手。</font><br>(非特指的)一(个)<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He works in a factory.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他在一家工厂工作。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp When I entered the room, I saw a man standing at the window.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我走进房间时, 看见一个男人站在窗前。</font><br>(同类事物中的)任何一(个)<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp A child needs love.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 儿童需要爱。</font><br>(用于表示时间、速度、价格等意义的)每一<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The boy was paid two dollars a day.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 那男孩每天挣两美元。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Apple costs five dollars a kilogram.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 苹果每千克五美元。</font><br>(用在某些物质名词和抽象名词前)一阵、一场、一种<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp A gentle wind disturbed the surface of the water.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 微风拂动水面。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He was caught in a heavy rain.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他遇上了一阵大雨。</font><br>\n
able	<h3>able</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adj.</i></font><br>能够…的, 得以…的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Most children are able to walk before they are able to talk.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 多数孩子在会说话前就会走路。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The patient was soon able to sit up.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 病人很快就能坐起来了。</font><br>有才干的, 有本事的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He was acknowledged as an able statesman.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他被公认为是个有才干的政治家。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The general impression at the studio was that he was able.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 在这个画室获得的总的印象是他很有才能。</font><br>\n
about	<h3>about</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>prep.</i></font><br>(表示位置)在…周围; 在…的各处; 在…的附近<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Fish are abundant about the reefs.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 暗礁附近鱼很多。</font><br>(表示对象)对, 对于<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I am very sorry about your troubles.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 对于你遇到的麻烦我非常遗憾。</font><br>(表示原因)由于, 因为<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp John is anxious about his exam results.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 约翰为考试结果而担忧。</font><br>(表示论及)关于; 涉及; 在…方面<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp What is the book about?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这本书是关于什么内容的?</font><br>(表示所属)属于, 体现在…身上<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp His face is the worst thing about him.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他吃亏就吃在他的面孔上。</font><br>(表示过程)忙于, 从事<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Henry's gone a long time. I wonder what he's about.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 亨利去了很长时间了, 我不知道他在干什么。</font><br>(表示伴随)在身边<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Do you happen to have his letter about you?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 你是否正好带着他的信了?</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adv.</i></font><br>大约, 差不多<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She died about two years ago.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她大约在两年前就死了。</font><br>在四周, 处处<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He lay asleep with his clothes scattered about.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他躺着睡了, 脱下的衣服四处放着。</font><br>在附近<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Nobody seemed about, so I went in.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 附近好像没人, 于是我就进去了。</font><br>\n
accept	<h3>accept</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt. & vi.</i></font><br>接受, 领受, 收受<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp If you accept, please let me know.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 如果你接受的话, 请通知我。</font><br>承担责任; 承兑<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The firm accepted personal cheques.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这家公司承兑私人支票。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt.</i></font><br>承认, 同意; 认为, 相信<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Please accept me as a friend.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 请把我当作朋友。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The police accepted his story as true.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 警察对他的话信以为真。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He accepted me as having seen the much of the world.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他承认我见识广。</font><br>\n
accord	<h3>accord</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>一致, 符合<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp They came to an accord that profits should be shared equally.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们达成协议, 收益由大家均分。</font><br>(尤指国与国之间的)谅解, 协议<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The government expected a temporary accord with the Opposition before the end of the year.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 政府期望年底以前和反对党达成临时协议。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt.</i></font><br>给予, 赠予<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp We accorded the boy due praise.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们给了孩子适当的表扬。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The committee accorded a scholarship to her.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 委员会批准给她奖学金。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vi.</i></font><br>符合, 一致<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The two statements accord superficially.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这两项声明表面上一致。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Most of my classmates accord in that opinion.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们班大多数同学都是那个意见。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp His story accords with what I saw.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他讲的与我看到的是吻合的。</font><br>\n
according to	<h3>according to</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>prep.</i></font><br>(表示依据)根据, 按照<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp You've been in prison three times according to our records.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 根据我们的记录, 你曾入狱三次。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Fill up the form according to the instructions.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 按照说明将表填好。</font><br>\n
account	<h3>account</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>账, 账户<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The sum of money has been transferred into my account.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 那笔钱已转到我账上。</font><br>记述, 描述, 报道<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The two accounts of the accident do not agree.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 有关这次事件两则报道不一致。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vi.</i></font><br>解释; 说明<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp His illness accounts for his absence.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他因为生病, 所以才缺席。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He has to account to the chairman for how he spends the company's money.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他一定要向主席说明他是如何花公司的钱的。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt.</i></font><br>认为<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp We all account him a qualified teacher.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们都认为他是一名合格的教师。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Tom accounts himself (to be) lucky.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 汤姆认为自己运气好。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He accounted it fun to go to sea.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他认为去海边很有趣。</font><br>\n
across	<h3>across</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>prep.</i></font><br>(表示位置)在…对面[另一边]; 横在[披在]…上; 掠过…; 透过<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp There's a hotel across the road.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 路的另一边有一家旅馆。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She was wearing a silver fox fur across her shoulders.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她肩上披了一张银狐皮。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp A smile of pleasure passed across his face.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他脸上掠过一丝快乐的微笑。</font><br>(表示方向)横越, 横跨; 横穿, 穿越; 从…的另一面[边]<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp A straight line was ruled across the map.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 一条直线横划在地图上。</font><br>(表示状态)与…交叉着; 触及, 波及, 影响到<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp This policy stretches across several different departments.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这项政策影响着几个不同的部门。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adv.</i></font><br>从这一边到另一边<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He turned his head and looked across at me.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他转过头, 打量着我。</font><br>在对面, 向对面<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp We leave Dover at ten and we should be across in France by midnight.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 十点钟离开多佛的话, 我们午夜时分可以到达对面的法国。</font><br>跨度<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The river is half a mile across.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 江面宽半英里。</font><br>成十字形, 成交叉状<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He sat there quietly, with his arms across.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他双臂交叉, 静静地坐在那儿。</font><br>传达过来<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He began to talk, slipping the words across.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他开始讲话, 轻声把字吐出来。</font><br>\n
act	<h3>act</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt. & vi.</i></font><br>行动, 做<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The time for thinking is past, we must now act.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 思考的时间过去了, 我们现在必须行动。</font><br>表演, 假装<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Oliver is acting tonight.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 奥利弗今晚演出。</font><br>起作用<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The medicine acts well.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这药有效。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>行为, 行动<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp My first act was to run into the waiting room.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我的第一个行动就是跑进客厅。</font><br>法令, 条例<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The drug was banned by an act of parliament.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 议会的法案明令禁止该药品。</font><br>(一)幕<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Most modern plays have three acts.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 大多数现代戏剧有三幕。</font><br>\n
action	<h3>action</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>行动, 活动<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The time has come for action.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 行动的时候到了。</font><br>所做之事, 行为<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He was sorry for his actions.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他为自己的行为感到懊悔。</font><br>情节<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The action is set in France.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 事情发生在法国。</font><br>作用, 功能<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Photographs are produced by the action of light on film.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 光对底片发生作用从而产生照片。</font><br>\n
actually	<h3>actually</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adv.</i></font><br>实际上, 确实<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Actually, Grandpa was over 70.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 实际上祖父已70多岁。</font><br>\n
after	<h3>after</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>prep.</i></font><br>(表示时间)在…以后<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp After the play they called for the author to show himself.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 剧终之后他们请求编剧和大家见面。</font><br>(表示位置、顺序)在…后面<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The King came in, with all his servants following after him.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 国王走了进来, 所有侍从跟在他的后面。</font><br>(表示原因)由于, 鉴于<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She succeeded in solving the problem after hard work.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 由于努力干, 她终于解决了那个问题。</font><br>(表示条件)与…一致; 符合<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He was built after his father.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他的体型像父亲。</font><br>(表示方式)像, 仿照<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp This box is made after a new pattern.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这箱子是仿照新样式制作的。</font><br>(表示依据)以…之名命名<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The boy was named Tom after his grandfather.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这小孩按他祖父的名字被起名为汤姆。</font><br>(表示论及)关于; 涉及<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He inquired after your health.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他询问你的健康状况。</font><br>(表示目标)追求, 追寻<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp There were always lots of men after her because she was clever as well as pretty.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 总有许多男人追求她, 因为她既漂亮又聪明。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I wonder what those children are after in that shed.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我不知道那些孩子在棚子里寻找什么。</font><br>(表示让步)尽管, 仍然<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp After all my advice, he still went his own way.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 在我苦口婆心地相劝后, 他仍然一意孤行。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>conj.</i></font><br>在…以后<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp After he goes, we shall eat.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他走之后, 我们就吃饭。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adv.</i></font><br>以后, 继后<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp They arrived soon after.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们没多久就到达了。</font><br>\n
again	<h3>again</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adv.</i></font><br>再(次), 又(一次)<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp It's good to see all my teachers and friends again.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 又见到我的老师和朋友们真是好极了。</font><br>此外, 另一方面<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp And again, can you acknowledge it as true?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 再者, 你会认为真有此事吗?</font><br>反响, 反应<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp You will be loved again.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 你的爱定会得到回报。</font><br>\n
against	<h3>against</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>prep.</i></font><br>(表示方向)与…方向相反, 逆着, 迎着, 顶着<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp You should fly your kite against the wind.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 你应该迎着风放风筝。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She always advances against difficulties.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她总是迎着困难上。</font><br>(表示方位)紧靠着…, 倚靠着…<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The seats have no back against which to lean.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这些座位都没有靠背可倚。</font><br>(表示对象)对…不利, 对…有害; 和…碰撞, 与…撞击; 预防, 以…为抵御对象; 以…为竞争对手; 违反, 违背<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The present economic climate works against the smaller companies.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 当前的经济气候对小公司不利。</font><br>(表示目的)为…做准备, 防备…之用<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She is preparing a substantial meal against his return.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她正在准备一顿丰盛的饭菜为他接风。</font><br>(表示态度)反对, 反抗<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He fought against the disease for a long time.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他同疾病做了长时间的斗争。</font><br>(表示依据)以…为标准<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I checked my watch against the steeple clock.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我根据教堂尖塔的大钟对了表。</font><br>以…兑换, 以…交换<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Please deliver this package against payment of cost.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 请把这件货物送去, 把货款带回。</font><br>(表示对比)和…比, 和…对照; 以…为背景<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He is elected by a majority of 40 votes against 10.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他以40票对10票的大多数票当选。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The mountain looks magnificent against the sky.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 在蓝天的衬托下, 这座山显得雄伟壮丽。</font><br>\n
age	<h3>age</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>年龄, 年纪<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp They married at a late age.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们年龄很大时才结婚。</font><br>老年, 老<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp You have something to learn in youth and in age.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 年轻和年老都有东西可学。</font><br>时代, 时期<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The sage is the instructor of a hundred ages.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这位哲人是百代之师。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt. & vi.</i></font><br>(使)长大, 变老<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp After his wife's death, he aged quickly.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 妻子死后, 他老得很快。</font><br>\n
ago	<h3>ago</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adv.</i></font><br>以前<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I realized it three weeks ago.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我在三个星期以前才明白的。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp How long ago is it that you last saw her?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 你上次看见她是多久以前?</font><br>\n
agree	<h3>agree</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt. & vi.</i></font><br>同意, 赞同<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I asked him to come with me and he agreed.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我请他和我一起来, 他同意了。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp We must agree the arrangements for this.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们必须接受为此所作的安排。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp They agreed to reserve four tickets for us.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们答应给我们留四张票。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vi.</i></font><br>相同, 相符, 一致<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The essential thing is that the two of you ought to agree.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 根本的问题是你们俩应意见一致。</font><br>(气候、食物等)适宜, 相和<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp These two shades do not agree.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这两种色调不协调。</font><br>\n
aid	<h3>aid</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt.</i></font><br>帮助, 援助<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp They aided the poor.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们帮助穷人。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>帮助, 援助, 救助<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He went to the aid of the hurt man.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他前去帮助那受伤的人。</font><br>助手, 辅助物, 辅助手段<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He was a doctor's aid for a time.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他一度做过一名大夫的助手。</font><br>\n
air	<h3>air</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>天空, 大气, 空气; 气氛<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp We breathe air.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们呼吸空气。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp There was an air of excitement at the meeting.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 会议上气氛激昂。</font><br>空中<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Many birds are flying in the air.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 许多鸟儿在空中飞翔。</font><br>样子, 神态, 姿态<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp They were displeased with her haughty airs.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们讨厌她高傲的派头。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt. & vi.</i></font><br>晾晒, 烘干<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The straw mattresses are airing there.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 草垫子正在那里晾着。</font><br>播送, 广播<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The program airs daily.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 本节目每天广播。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt.</i></font><br>使房间通风, 透气<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp We air the room by opening the windows.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们打开窗子让屋子通风。</font><br>\n
all	<h3>all</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adj.</i></font><br>一切的, 所有的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp All the children are not noisy.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 并不是所有的儿童都吵闹。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp All his toys cannot make him happy.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 即使他的全部玩具也不能使他快乐。</font><br>全部的, 总的, 整个的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp All my flowers have died.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我的花全死了。</font><br>尽量的, 极度的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp All five men are hard workers.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们五个人工作都很努力。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>pron.</i></font><br>全部; 一切<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp All were silent.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 大家都不吭声。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp All of us were disappointed by him.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他使我们大家都失望了。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adv.</i></font><br>完全地, 很<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She was dressed all in white.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她从头到脚一身白。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He was all excited.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他非常兴奋。</font><br>\n
allow	<h3>allow</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt.</i></font><br>允许, 许可(做某事)<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I don't think he would allow it.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我想他不会允许的。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Do they allow smoking in the cinemas?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们允许在电影院里抽烟吗?</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Allow me to introduce you to our headmaster.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 请允许我介绍你见见我们的校长。</font><br>给予, 让…得到<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The court allowed a sum of money to each child for clothing.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 法院判给每个孩子一笔服装费。</font><br>承认, 认为<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The referee refused to allow the goal.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 裁判不承认这次进球。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp You must allow yourself to be wrong.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 你必须承认自己错了。</font><br>\n
almost	<h3>almost</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adv.</i></font><br>几乎, 差不多, 差一点; 将近<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp In his blind haste he almost ran into the river.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他匆匆忙忙地几乎跑到河里去了。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp In the hall it was almost dark.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 大厅里几乎漆黑一片。</font><br>\n
along	<h3>along</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adv.</i></font><br>向前, 往前<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The policeman told the crowds to move along.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 警察叫人群向前走。</font><br>一道, 一起<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Come to the party and bring some friends along.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 请来参加聚会并带些朋友来。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>prep.</i></font><br>(表示位置)沿着…的某地点; 在…旁的某地方<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp His room is along this passage.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他的房间在这条通道上。</font><br>(表示方向)沿着, 循着, 顺着<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I took my dog for a walk along the river.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我带着狗沿那条河散步。</font><br>(表示方位)靠着<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp There is a striped sofa along the wall.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 有一张靠墙放着的有条纹的沙发。</font><br>(表示依据)根据, 顺着<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Here are a few suggestions along this line.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这是根据这一路线提出的一些意见。</font><br>\n
already	<h3>already</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adv.</i></font><br>早已, 已经<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He had already left when I called.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我打电话去时, 他已走了。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp When I came in, she was already laying the table.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我进来时, 她已在摆餐具了。</font><br>\n
also	<h3>also</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adv.</i></font><br>也, 同样, 并且<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp You'll have to get a passport, and you'll also need a visa.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 你必须申办护照, 同时还需要有签证。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I am also writing a short story.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我也写短篇小说。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The son has gone also.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 儿子也去了。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She not only plays well, but also writes music.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她不仅很会演奏, 而且还会作曲。</font><br>\n
although	<h3>although</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>conj.</i></font><br>尽管, 虽然<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Although my car is very old, it still runs very well.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我的汽车虽然很旧, 但仍然跑得很快。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Although they are poor they are happy.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 虽然他们很穷, 但很快乐。</font><br>但是, 然而<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The high tax policy is certainly unpopular, although it's unlikely to meet the soaring armament expenditures.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 高赋税政策肯定是不受欢迎的，但也未必能满足飞涨的军备开支。</font><br>\n
always	<h3>always</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adv.</i></font><br>总是; 永远; 一直; 无例外地<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He always acts the lord.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他总是装阔。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp You've always been my close friend.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 你一直是我亲密的朋友。</font><br>重复地; 有规律地<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp My little daughter is always bothering me when I'm at work.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我工作时, 我的小女儿老爱打扰我。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She is not always late.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她有时迟到。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Freddie almost[nearly] always goes to town on Sunday nights.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 弗雷迪几乎每星期天晚上都进城。</font><br>\n
among	<h3>among</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>prep.</i></font><br>(表示位置)处在…中, 为…所环绕, 为…所环抱<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He was sitting among a group of children, telling them a story.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他正坐在一群孩子中间讲故事。</font><br>(表示方式)以…联合行动<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp They earned a fortune among themselves.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们共同努力发了财。</font><br>(表示比较)与…比较, 突出于<br>(表示排斥)除…之外(还有)<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The conference discussed, among other things, the problem of environmental protection.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 除了其他问题以外，会上还讨论了环保问题。</font><br>(表示范围)在…之内, 为…所分享[共有], 在…一类之中, 是…中之一, 在…群中<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She is the tallest among her classmates.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她在她同学之中是最高的。</font><br>(表示环境)与…在一起, 与…相处<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp My wife was there among others.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我妻子和其他一些人在那儿。</font><br>(表示牵涉)经过, 涉及<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Unemployment among married women reached a peak.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 在已婚女性中失业率达到了顶峰。</font><br>(表示关系)相互间, 彼此<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp You must settle the matter among yourselves.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 你们必须彼此商量, 自行解决这些问题。</font><br>(表示所属)为…所特有; 为…所熟悉<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp This is a custom among the Germans.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这是德国人特有的习俗。</font><br>\n
and	<h3>and</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>conj.</i></font><br>和, 与, 及<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He likes to play football and to sing popular songs.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他喜欢踢足球和唱流行歌曲。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp There are three hundred and sixty-five students in this school.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这所学校有365个学生。</font><br>那么, 则<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He lost his health, and therefore his difficulties increased.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他身体虚弱, 因此更增加了他的困难。</font><br>然后, 接着<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp It came nearer and nearer.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 那东西越来越近了。</font><br>而且, 还, 又<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Mary was tall and fair.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 玛丽是个高个子的金发女郎。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Joan was rich, beautiful and proud.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 琼非常有钱, 漂亮且庄重。</font><br>\n
announce	<h3>announce</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt. & vi.</i></font><br>宣布, 宣告, 发表<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp They announced that a cold wave would come soon.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们报告说不久寒流就要来。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Have they announced when the race will begin?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们宣布比赛什么时候开始了吗?</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp A voice on the phone announced itself as Mr. Baker.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 电话里的人说他是贝克先生。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp “I've a proposal to make, ” she announced as she entered.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她一进来就对大家说“我有个建议。”</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt.</i></font><br>通报…到达<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Would you announce the guests as they come in?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 客人来时你通报一声好吗?</font><br>预告, 预示<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The bright flowers and warm winds announced that spring was here.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 鲜艳的花朵和暖和的风已表明春天到了。</font><br>主持, 介绍<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The inauguration of the President is announced for Friday.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 总统的就职典礼已定于星期五举行。</font><br>\n
another	<h3>another</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adj.</i></font><br>又一个, 再一个<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp That boy will be another Nelson.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 那个男孩将成为尼尔逊第二。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Have another piece of cake.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 请再来块蛋糕。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp They had three goals in the first half, and another two in the second.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们在上半场进了三个球, 下半场又进了两个。</font><br>另一的, 其他一种<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Look at the difficulty in another way.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 用另一种不同的观点看待困难。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp That's quite another matter.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 那完全是另外一回事。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>pron.</i></font><br>另一个, 别个<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I don't like this one, show me another.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我不喜欢这个, 请让我看看另一个。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp It is just such another.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这真是无独有偶。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp You will never see such another.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 那样的人物恐怕再也看不到了。</font><br>再一个<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp If you take one glass, you will take another and another.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 如果你喝了第一杯, 你就会一杯接一杯地喝下去。</font><br>\n
answer	<h3>answer</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt. & vi.</i></font><br>答复; 解答; 答辩<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I asked him a question but he would not answer.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我问了他一个问题, 但是他不作回答。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I telephoned this afternoon, but nobody answered.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我今天下午打过电话, 但没人接。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He answered that he knew nothing about it.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他回答说关于此事他一无所知。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He answered, “It's two o'clock.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp ”他回答说“现在两点。”</font><br>适应, 符合, 满足<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp It answers very well.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这完全适用。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Our work must answer the specifications laid down.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们的工作应符合所定的规范。</font><br>回应, 响应<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The workers answered by calling a strike.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 工人举行罢工进行回击。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Three fire companies answered the alarm.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 听到警报后, 三个消防队都来了。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>回答; 回音<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Facts are the best answers.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 事实是最好的回答。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp We often learn foreign language through questions and answers.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们常用问答的方式学外语。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Have you had an answer to your letter?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 你收到回信了吗?</font><br>答案<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp You can find the answers of all the exercises at the end of this book.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 在这本书后面, 你可以找到所有习题的答案。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp It's the answer to your question.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这就是你的问题的答案。</font><br>反应<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp A nod was her only answer.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 点了下头是她仅有的反应。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The publication comes as the answer to an acute demand.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这一出版物是为满足急需而出版的。</font><br>\n
any	<h3>any</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>pron.</i></font><br>无论哪个, 无论哪些<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He saved all the fish for his children and never tasted any himself.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他把鱼都留给孩子们, 自己一点都没有尝。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp This is the last chance any of us has.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 对于我们中的任何人来说, 这是最后的一次机会。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Their performance that night was better than any before.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们那天晚上的演出比以往任何一次都好。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adj.</i></font><br>任何一个(的)<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp China is larger than any country in Africa.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 中国比任何一个非洲国家都大。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp There are scarcely any flies left around there.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 那周围几乎没有任何苍蝇了。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp We got there without any trouble.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们顺利到达。</font><br>一点, 一些<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Haven't you any work to do?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 你有要干的活吗?</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Come and see me if you have any time.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 如有空就来看我。</font><br>普通的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp You can't just wear any clothes if you're going there—you have to dress very smartly.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 如果你去那里, 你不能穿着普普通通的衣服, 你必须穿得很整齐漂亮。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adv.</i></font><br>丝毫, 一点<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He was never any good.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他一向不行。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I couldn't stand it any longer.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我不能再忍受了。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He didn't want to express himself any more strongly than he had to.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他不想更强烈地表现自己。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I didn't like it any.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我压根就不喜欢它。</font><br>\n
anything	<h3>anything</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>pron.</i></font><br>无论什么东西, 随便什么事情<br>任何东西, 任何事情绝对不<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I want something to eat; anything will do.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我想吃点东西, 随便什么都行。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Is there anything wrong?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 有什么毛病吗?</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Do you know anything about that country?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 你对那个国家了解得多吗?</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Is he anything of a statesman?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他像个政治家吗?</font><br>\n
appear	<h3>appear</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vi.</i></font><br>出现, 显现<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp We expected him, but he never appeared.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们等他, 他却一直没来。</font><br>产生, 出版<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp This magazine will appear fortnightly.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这杂志将两周出一期。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>link v.</i></font><br>显得, 似乎<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp It appeared that he had a taste for music.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 看来他对音乐还有一定的鉴赏力。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She appeared not to have heard what he had said.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她似乎没有听见他的话。</font><br>\n
area	<h3>area</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>面积<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp What's the area of your garden?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 你的花园有多大面积?</font><br>区域, 地区<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp People in cold areas live longer.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 寒带地区的人寿命较长。</font><br>领域, 方面<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He proposed half a dozen accords in such areas as culture, post and communications.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他就文化、邮电和通讯领域提出了六项建议。</font><br>\n
arm	<h3>arm</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>臂<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He broke his arm in an accident.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他在一次事故中折断了手臂。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp There must be something wrong with my left arm, which is asleep.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我的左臂发麻, 一定出什么问题了。</font><br>武器, 军火<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp People were up in arms against the invaders.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 人民拿起武器反抗侵略者。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt. & vi.</i></font><br>(把…)武装起来<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Their former enemy is arming again.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们从前的敌人正在重整军备。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Arm yourselves and be ready to fight.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 武装起来, 准备战斗。</font><br>\n

around	<h3>around</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adv.</i></font><br>在周围, 在附近<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I can't see anyone around.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我看见附近一个人也没有。</font><br>到处, 四周<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I hear laughter all around.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我听到四周的笑声。</font><br>大约<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I'll be back at around 5 o'clock.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 五点左右我就回来。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>prep.</i></font><br>(表示位置)围绕, 绕在; 在…各处, 在…范围之内; 在…附近, 在…周围<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp They sat around the table.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们围着桌子坐。</font><br>(表示方向)绕过, 越过; 朝…的四周, 往…的四周<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Let's go around the town, not through it.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们从城外绕过去, 不要穿城而过。</font><br>(表示状态)包着, 裹着; 在…身边, 接近(某人)<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I bound the cloth around my head to stop the bleeding.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我将布裹在头上止血。</font><br>(表示依据)以…为中心, 根据<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Their society was built around a belief in God.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们的社会建立在信仰上帝的基础上。</font><br>\n
art	<h3>art</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>艺术, 美术<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She loves art.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她热爱美术。</font><br>技能, 技巧<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Driving a car in Central London needs quite an art!</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 在伦敦市中心开车可真需要点技术！</font><br>\n
as	<h3>as</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adv.</i></font><br>同样地, 一样地<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She is as tall as her mother.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她和她母亲一样高。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The dining room was twice as big as the Tom's.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这个餐厅比汤姆的餐厅大一倍。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp This is as difficult a problem as you are likely to meet.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 像这样的难题, 你可能会碰到。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>prep.</i></font><br>(表示时间)当还是…的时候<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp As a schoolboy, he showed every sign of genius.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 当他还是个小学生的时候, 就显示出了天资聪慧。</font><br>(表示方式)以…的身份, 以…资格, 作为; 以…形式, 以作为; 以…角色, 扮演…角色; 如同, 像<br>(表示结果)成为, 看作, 看成<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp We had better treat it as a joke.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们最好把它当作玩笑。</font><br>(表示目的)为了, 以…为目的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The dykes were built as a protection against the sea.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 建筑堤坝是为了防止海水泛滥。</font><br>(表示举例)例如, 诸如…之类的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp We talked about such subjects as the weather.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们谈论了诸如天气之类的话题。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>conj.</i></font><br>在…期间, 当…时候<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I was coming in as he was going out.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我进来的时候, 他正出去。</font><br>尽管, 即使, 虽然<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Intelligent as you are, I suspect you will fail.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 尽管你聪明, 我猜想你会失败。</font><br>像…一样<br>由于, 因为<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp As you weren't there I left a message.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 因为你不在那里, 我留了个信儿。</font><br>\n
ask	<h3>ask</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt. & vi.</i></font><br>问, 询问<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp If you don't know, you must ask.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 假如你不知道, 你就要问。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She asked how to mend the radio.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她问无线电怎么修。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp We ask you ten dollars.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们向你要价十美元。</font><br>要求, 请求<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I must ask to be excused.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我必须请求原谅。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He asked that they should be allowed to leave.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他请求允许他们离开。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt.</i></font><br>邀请<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp They were asked to attend the meeting.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们应邀出席会议。</font><br>\n
at	<h3>at</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>prep.</i></font><br>(表示位置) 在, 于; 到达, 达到; 经, 由; 在…旁, 靠近; 在…里; 在…上; 在…方位<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He was not at his office.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他不在办公室。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He was standing at the door.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他正站在门边。</font><br>(表示时间)在, 在…时刻[时辰, 期间, 阶段, 时节]; 在…岁时<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The meeting will open at 15 ∶ 00.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 会议在下午三点钟开始。</font><br>(表示状态)处于…状态, 在…情况下<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The soldiers are standing at attention.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 士兵们立正站着。</font><br>(表示方式)以…的方式; 通过一次…的动作<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I was there at a bound.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我纵身一跃就到了那里。</font><br>(表示原因)因为, 由于; 由于有, 由于应…<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp We were frightened at the terrible sight.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 看到这可怕的景象, 我们被吓呆了。</font><br>(表示距离)从, 在距离…处<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I saw it at a distance.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我从远处看见了它。</font><br>(表示目标)朝, 向, 对着<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He threw the key at me.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他把钥匙丢给我。</font><br>(表示环境)出席, 参加<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I remember him at a banquet on that night.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我记得那天晚上他参加了一个宴会。</font><br>(表示方向)在…方面<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She is good at describing things or expressing ideas.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她善于描述事物或表达思想。</font><br>\n
attack	<h3>attack</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt. & vi.</i></font><br>攻击, 进攻; 抨击<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp They knew when to attack and when to retreat.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们知道什么时候进攻和什么时候撤退。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The enemy attacked us at night.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 敌人在夜间袭击了我们。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>攻击, 袭击<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The enemy attack took us by surprise.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 敌人的进攻使我们感到意外。</font><br>抨击, 辱骂<br>(疾病)侵袭, 发作<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She had her first heart attack the other day.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 不久前, 她第一次心脏病发作。</font><br>\n

between	<h3>between</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>prep.</i></font><br>(表示位置)在…之间; 在…之中<br>(表示时间)在…与…的一段时间内; 在…的间隔中<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I will come between twelve and one o'clock.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我会在12点至1点之间来。</font><br>(表示数目)介乎…之间<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp We must have walked between ten and twelve miles.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们应该已步行了10至12英里。</font><br>(表示距离)在…到…的一段距离内, 来往于…与…之间<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp It is about thirty miles between Nottingham and Sheffield.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 从诺丁汉到谢菲尔德大约30英里。</font><br>(表示范围)在…之间, 为…所分享<br>(表示等级)介乎于…之间<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp An army major ranks between a captain and a colonel.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 陆军少校的军阶在上尉与中校之间。</font><br>(表示关系)在…之间; …与…之间; 涉及<br>(表示对比)从…中选择, 就…比较而言<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp There's nothing to choose between them.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 它们之间无可选择。</font><br>\n

进入…状态<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp One after another, all of them fell asleep.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 那些人一个接一个地睡着了。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Suddenly he fell ill and ran a high fever.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他突然病倒, 发起高烧。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He fell prey to her charms.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他被她的美色所迷倒。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>跌落, 下落<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He survived a fall of 40 feet.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他从40英尺高的地方跌下来没有丧命。</font><br>下降, 降低, 减少<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp There was a sudden fall in temperature.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 气温一下子降低了。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp There was a fall in the price of apples.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 苹果的价格下跌了。</font><br>掉落的距离, 落差<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp It's a fall of 60 metres to the foot of the cliff.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 从这儿到悬崖之底距离60米。</font><br>陷落; 努力获得<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp What do you find the total?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 你要求的总数是多少?</font><br>供给, 供应; 知道…是有的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I can't find that amount of money.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我不能提供那笔款子。</font><br>〈律〉判决, 裁决<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The jury found against the plaintiff.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 陪审团做出不利于原告的判决。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>发现<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp That old book is quite a find.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 那本古书是一个重大发现。</font><br>发现物<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The new finds have deepened our knowledge of giant ape.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 新的发现物加深了我们对巨猿的认识。</font><br>\n

from	<h3>from</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>prep.</i></font><br>(表示时间)从…, 自…<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp We've been working from morning to night.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们从早到晚一直工作。</font><br>(表示状态)从某(位置、状态等)开始<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He rose from office boy to managing director in ten years.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他在十年间由办公室勤杂员升至总经理。</font><br>(表示范围)从较低限度算起<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The jackets are from 35 dollars.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这些夹克衫起价是35美元。</font><br>(表示来源)来自…; 源于…; 从…里取出<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I come from the north.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我是北方人。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He took a shaving mirror from his bag.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他从手提包里拿出一面剃须镜。</font><br>(表示分离)与…分离[隔开]; 减去; 扣除<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The wind blew his hat from his head.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 风将他的帽子从头上吹走了。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Six from fifteen leaves nine.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 15减6等于9。</font><br>(表示否定)免于; 免遭<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Wild fruit kept us from dying of starvation.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们靠着野果才没被饿死。</font><br>(表示方位)从…; 以…为开始方向<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Latitudes are the lines that go from east to west.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 纬线是从东到西的线。</font><br>(表示原因)因为, 出于<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She told him the truth from a sense of loyalty.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她告诉他真相是出于忠诚。</font><br>(表示比较)与…相比; 与…区分<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She is different from her sister in character.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她和她姐姐性格不同。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He can tell a fake from the original.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他能分辨出赝品和真品。</font><br>\n
front	<h3>front</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>前面; 正面<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Sweeping all others aside, she pushed her way to the front.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她把别人都推开, 挤到了前边。</font><br>一面<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The west front of the church contains some fine old windows.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这教堂的西侧有一些精美的旧式窗户。</font><br>前线, 战线<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The main body of troops moved toward the front.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 主力部队开往前线。</font><br>联合行动, 阵线<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The opposition parties can only defeat the government if they present a united front.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 所有反对党只有结成联合阵线才能击败政府。</font><br>幌子, 隐蔽物<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Although he was very nervous, he put on a brave front.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 尽管他非常紧张, 但还是装出一副勇敢的样子。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp This firm is just a front for their illegal trade in diamonds.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这家公司不过是他们进行非法钻石交易的一个幌子。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adj.</i></font><br>前面的, 前部的; 正面的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The wardrobe in the front bedroom has been built in.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 前面卧室里的衣橱已经镶建在墙壁之内了。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt.</i></font><br>作…的正面<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Imported marble will front the building.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这建筑物的正面将用进口的大理石来装饰。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt. & vi.</i></font><br>面向, 朝向<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The cinema fronts toward the south.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 电影院朝南。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The hotel fronts on the main road.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 旅馆朝向大马路。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The hotel fronts the beautiful lake.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这家旅馆面对着那美丽的湖。</font><br>\n
full	<h3>full</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adj.</i></font><br>满的, 装满的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The train was crowded to its full capacity.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 火车上挤满了乘客。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp It is rude to speak with your mouth full.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 满嘴含着东西讲话很不礼貌。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The car was full but I squeezed in any way.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 汽车已经满人了, 但是我还是设法挤了进去。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp My basket is so full that I can't carry it.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我的篮子装得太满, 我拿不动它。</font><br>完全的, 充分的, 完整的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Only full members of the club are allowed to vote at meeting.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 只有俱乐部的正式会员才可以在会中投票。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He has been away for a full year now.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他离开已整整一年了。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp A comprehensive description is one that is full and complete.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 一篇详尽的描写就是一篇充实完整的描写。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He was full on that point.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他对那一点讲得很详尽。</font><br>\n
fund	<h3>fund</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>基金, 专款<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp We made a contribution to the famine relief fund.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们给饥荒赈济基金捐了款。</font><br>现款; 资金<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She is willing to help, but she's out of funds at present.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她愿意帮助, 但目前她拿不出现金。</font><br>储备, 蕴藏<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He has a fund of amusing jokes.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他有很多有趣的笑话。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt.</i></font><br>为…提供资金, 给…拨款<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The company is funding another scheme.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这个公司正为另一项计划拨款。</font><br>\n
further	<h3>further</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adj.</i></font><br>更多的, 另外的, 进一步的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp If you wish for further explanation, you'd better apply in person to the director.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 如果你想得到进一步说明, 你最好直接找厂长联系。</font><br>更远的, 较远的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The desk is placed at the further end of the room.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 书桌摆在房间里较远的一头。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The church is much further than you think.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 教堂比你想像的远得多。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adv.</i></font><br>在更大程度上, 进一步地<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She refused to further talk that evening of her own worry.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 那天晚上她拒绝进一步说她的担忧。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The house isn't big enough for us, and further, it's too far from the town.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 那住宅对我们来说不够大, 而且离城又太远。</font><br>更远, 再往前地<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He can swim further than I can.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他能游得比我远。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The village is about two miles further on.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 再向前约两英里就是那个村庄。</font><br>此外, 而且<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Further, it has come to my attention.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 此外, 我已注意到它了。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt.</i></font><br>促进, 推进, 助长<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp We'll do all we can to further your plans.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们将尽力促成你们的计划。</font><br>\n

game	<h3>game</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>游戏<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp They are playing a game of cards.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们在玩牌。</font><br>运动, 比赛<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The football game is yours.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这场足球赛你们胜了。</font><br>一场, 一局, 一盘<br><i><font played off seven games against each other.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 各组的前几名彼此进行七场比赛。</font><br>运动会<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The 1984 Olympic Games was held 狮子和老虎是大猎物。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adj.</i></font><br>勇敢的, 有决心的, 敢作敢当的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He was a game fighter even when he was losing.</font></i><br><font 她敢冒任何风险。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He is game for anything no matter how dangerous it is.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 无论这件事有多么危险, 他都敢去做。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The little boy was hurt by the fall, but he was game enough to get up and try again.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这个小男孩跌倒受伤了, 但他非常勇敢地站起来, 准备再试一试。</font><br>愿意的, 心甘情愿的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp “Who's game for a swim?”“I'm game!”</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp “谁愿意去游泳?”“我愿意!”</font><br>残疾的; 瘸的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The camel has a game leg.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 那只骆驼有一只腿瘸。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He is game in the left leg.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他左腿瘸。</font><br>\n
general	<h3>general</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adj.</i></font><br>普遍的, 全面的; 总体的, 整体的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The general opinion is in favour of us.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 舆论普遍对我们有利。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp These difficulties are general among people of his age.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这些困难在他那个年龄的人中普遍存在。</font><br>非专门的, 一般的<br>正常的, 常规的; 通常的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The serum is available to the general public.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 一般公众均可获得血清。</font><br>大致的, 笼统的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I have a general idea of how a car works.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我对汽车怎样工作有一个大致的了解。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Your answer is too general.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 你的答案太笼统。</font><br>总的, 首席的<br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>将军<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The general assigned him to do the tough task.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 将军派他去完成这项艰巨的任务。</font><br>\n
get	<h3>get</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt.</i></font><br>得到, 收到<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I've got your telegram.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 听到, 学得<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Did you get what I mean?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 你明白我的意思了吗?</font><br>感染上, 得(病)<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 那样我们不可能有任何进展。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp You'll get nowhere if you follow his instruction.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 要是你按他的方法去做, 将会一事无成。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp They tried to talk, but not knowing each other's language they didn't get far.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们试图交谈, labour	<h3>labour</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>劳动, 努力; 工作<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp They live by honest labour.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们靠正当劳动生活。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp This education aimed at combining brain work with manual labour.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 此项教育的目的在于实现脑力劳动与体力劳动相结合。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp We should try to reform criminals through labour rather than punish them.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们应该尽量通过劳动改造罪犯, 而不是惩罚他们。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp We regard labour as a matter of honour.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们认为劳动是光荣的事。</font><br>劳工, 工人<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Farm labour used to hire themselves out for the summer.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 农业工人过去经常整个夏天在外面打工。</font><br>分娩, (分娩时的)阵痛<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp His wife is in labour.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他的夫人正在分娩。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She was in labour for two hours before her baby was finally born.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她分娩了两个小时, 才生下婴儿。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She went into labour two weeks early.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她提前两周分娩了。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vi.</i></font><br>劳动; 努力<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The boy laboured quietly.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这个男孩静静地干着。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I laboured to understand him.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我努力了解他的意思。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp They have laboured to complete the job.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们努力完成这一工作。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp We laboured hard to finish our job ahead of schedule.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们努力工作, 以期把活儿提前干完。</font><br>艰难行进<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp They laboured along the bad road.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们在那条难走的路上艰难地行进。</font><br>\n

match	<h3>match</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>比赛, 竞赛<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp We had a friendly match with them.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们与他们进行了一场友谊比赛。</font><br>对手, 敌手<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Bill is no match for his younger brother at chess.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 比尔下棋不是他弟弟的对手。</font><br>相似之物, 相配之物<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The chairs and the desk are a good match.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这些椅子和这种书桌很相配。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The hat is a match for the coat.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这帽子与外衣很相配。</font><br>婚姻; 婚姻对象<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Both her daughters made good matches.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她两个女儿的婚姻都很美满。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt.</i></font><br>使较量, 使比赛<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp No one matches him when it comes to swimming.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 谈到游泳, 没有人比得过他。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt. & vi.</i></font><br>(使)相配; (使)相称<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Those two shoes don't match.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 那两只鞋不是一双。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The colours match well.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 颜色很协调。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The tie matches your suit.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 那条领带跟你的西装很相配。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He promised to match me a piece of cloth.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他答应过替我找一块布料来配。</font><br>\n
matter	<h3>matter</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>物质, 物体<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Matter is the opposite of mind.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 物质与精神相对。</font><br>题材, 内容<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The matter in your essay is good but the style is deplorable.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 你文章的内容很好, 但是体裁太糟糕了。</font><br>事情; 问题<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp This is a matter I know little about.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这件事我不太知道。</font><br>困难, 毛病, 麻烦<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp You must have something the matter with your eyes.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 你的眼睛一定有点毛病。</font><br>重要性<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp People know that and recognize its matter.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 人们知道这一点, 也认识到它的重要性。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vi.</i></font><br>要紧, 有关系<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp It does not matter at all.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 毫无关系。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp It doesn't matter throwing that away.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 把它扔掉, 没关系。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp It never mattered what time of day or night it was.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 不论是白天还是晚上, 都没有关系。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp It doesn't matter much whether we go together or separately.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们一起去还是分头去都可以。</font><br>\n
meet	<h3>meet</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt. & vi.</i></font><br>遇见, 碰见, 相见<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp We write regularly but seldom meet.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们经常通信, 却很少见面。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Glad to meet you.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 很高兴见到你。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I met her walking with John.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我碰见她和约翰走在一起。</font><br>认识, 结识<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I know her by sight, but we've never met.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我跟她只是面熟, 但并不认识。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Come to dinner to meet my sister.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 来参加晚宴, 认识一下我妹妹。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt.</i></font><br>迎接<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He hurried forward to meet them.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他快步向前去迎接他们。</font><br>满足<br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>运动会, 比赛<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp We have a sports meet every year.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们每年都开运动会。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I went to a swimming meet last night.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 昨天晚上我去看了游泳比赛。</font><br>\n
meeting	<h3>meeting</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>相会, 聚会, 会见<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp It was an accidental meeting.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这完全是一次偶然的相会。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp We have two meetings in London.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们在伦敦有两次聚会。</font><br>会议<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He spoke at the meeting in a bright voice.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他在会上大声地发言。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp They talked in the meeting.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们在会议期间私下谈话。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp What has the meeting decided?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 与会者做出了什么决定?</font><br>运动会<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp There is a sports meeting next week.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 下周有一场运动会。</font><br>\n
member	<h3>member</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>成员, 会员<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Every member of the organization should be constant to its regulations.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这组织的成员都得遵守规则。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He is a conservative member of the church.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他是一个守旧教会教友。</font><br>\n
middle	<h3>middle</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>中部, 中间<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp It's best to slice into a rich cake from the middle.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 最好把甜美的蛋糕从中间切开。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adj.</i></font><br>中部的; 中间的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I noticed two middle-aged passengers.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我注意到两个中年乘客。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He has three children, the middle child is a boy.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他有三个孩子, 老二是个男孩。</font><br>\n
military	<h3>military</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adj.</i></font><br>军事的, 军用的; 军人的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp My sister works in a military hospital.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我姐姐在一家部队医院工作。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp His bearing was very military.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他很有军人气概。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>军人; 军队, 武装力量<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp As the police could not keep order in the city, the military were called in to help.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 由于警察无法维持城里的秩序, 所以军队被召去加以协助。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The military has controlled the government.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 军人已经控制政府。</font><br>\n

minister	<h3>minister</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>大臣, 部长<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The newspaper reporters interviewed the minister.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 新闻记者们采访了这位部长。</font><br>公使, 外交使节<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He was the Chinese minister to Japan.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他曾是中国驻日本公使。</font><br>牧师<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp His original intention was to become a minister.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他原先的打算是当牧师。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vi.</i></font><br>辅助; 服侍<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He became a rector of a small parish where he ministered for several years.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他成为一个小教区的教区牧师, 在那里主事了几年圣事。</font><br>\n
