more	<h3>more</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adv.</i></font><br>更, 更加<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She read the letter more carefully the second time.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她第二次看信时更仔细了。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He is the more diligent of the two boys.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他是这两个男孩中较用功的一个。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adj.</i></font><br>更多的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp His behaviour did more harm than good to himself.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他的行为对他自己害多利少。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>pron.</i></font><br>更多的量<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp More of the land is planted to cabbages than to tomatoes.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 种白菜的地比种西红柿的多。</font><br>\n
morning	<h3>morning</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>早晨, 上午<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp At early morning I went up through the hillside woods.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 清晨我穿越山坡的小树林。</font><br>\n
most	<h3>most</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adv.</i></font><br>最<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp It was the most exciting holiday I've ever had.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 那是我经历过的最令人兴奋的假日。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Of course you're the most aristocratic of the two of us.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 你当然是我们两个人中最有贵族气派的。</font><br>很, 非常<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He spoke most bitterly of his experiences in prison.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他非常痛苦地讲述了他在监狱中的经历。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>pron.</i></font><br>大多数, 大部分<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp We spend most of March ploughing.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 三月份的大部分时间我们都在春耕。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Most of her books were stolen.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她的大部分书都被偷走了。</font><br>最高额; 最大值<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Do the most you can.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 尽你最大的力量去做。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adj.</i></font><br>最大的, 最多的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Peter made the most mistakes of all the class.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 全班同学中, 彼得出的错最多。</font><br>\n
mother	<h3>mother</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>母亲, 妈妈<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Your mother wouldn't like it if you become too thick with each other.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 如果你们来往太亲密, 你的母亲会不高兴的。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Old Mother Adams next door has lost her cat again.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 隔壁亚当斯老大娘的猫又不见了。</font><br>根由, 根源<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp School is the mother of learning.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 学校是知识的源泉。</font><br>\n
move	<h3>move</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt. & vi.</i></font><br>移动; 搬动<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Nobody moves.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 谁也不许动。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He is going to move his furniture.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他打算把家具移动一下位置。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vi.</i></font><br>搬家, 迁移<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp We are moving next week.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们下星期搬家。</font><br>进展, 前进, 展开<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The work moves slowly.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 工作进展缓慢。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt.</i></font><br>使感动, 激起<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The news moved him very much.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这消息使他很感动。</font><br>提议, 要求<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I move that we adopt the agenda as it stands.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我提议不作改变通过这个议程。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>动, 移动<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The snake made a small move.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 蛇稍微动了一下。</font><br>一步, 一着<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp One careless move loses the whole game.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 一着不慎, 全盘皆输。</font><br>行动, 行动步骤<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Unless we make a move soon, we shall not be able to fulfill our plan.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 如果不赶快采取行动, 我们就不能完成计划了。</font><br>迁移, 搬家<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp We'll make a move to the city next week.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们下星期要搬家到这个城市来。</font><br>\n
much	<h3>much</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adv.</i></font><br>非常, 很, 十分<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The car was too much damaged.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这部车损坏得太严重。</font><br>差不多, 几乎<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The dress is much the most expensive.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这件衣服差不多是最贵的。</font><br>很多地, 很大地, 程度极高地<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp You have much more confidence.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 你有更大的信心。</font><br>很大程度上, 常常<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Do you dine out much?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 你常常在外面进餐吗?</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adj.</i></font><br>许多的, 大量的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I have got far too much work to do.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我要做的事太多了。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>pron.</i></font><br>很多, 大量, 很大程度<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Jack had drunk too much in the party.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 杰克在晚会上喝得太多了。</font><br>很好的东西<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp We learned much from the experience.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们从这一经验中学到很多东西。</font><br>\n
music	<h3>music</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>音乐<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He was a great deal interested in music.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他对音乐非常感兴趣。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I like the idiom of modern popular music.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我喜欢现代流行音乐的风格。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I listened to the music on the radio.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我收听广播中播放的音乐。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp They waltz to the tempo of the music.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们跟着音乐的节奏跳华尔兹舞。</font><br>音乐作品, 乐曲<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He read the words and decided to write new music for them.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他读后决定为这首词谱写一个新曲子。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Many people like his music.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 许多人喜欢他的乐曲。</font><br>乐谱<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I'd left my music at home.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我把乐谱落在家里了。</font><br>\n
must	<h3>must</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>aux.v.</i></font><br>必须<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp If you can't finish the book by then, you must come and renew it.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这本书如果你到时候还看不完, 就必须来续借。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The children must be back by 4 o'clock.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 孩子们必须四点钟以前回来。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp You must remember to write home.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 你必须记着给家里写信。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp We mustn't waste our time.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们不应该浪费时间。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp “May I take this magazine out?”“No, you mustn't.”</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp “我可以把这本杂志借走吗?”“不, 不行。”</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He said he must go tomorrow.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他说他明天必须去。</font><br>必然要, 必定会<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp We must all die.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 人都是要死的。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp How long must this go on?What's the sense of this?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这种局势要持续多久呢?它有什么意义呢?</font><br>(做出逻辑推断)<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He must be mad.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他一定是疯了。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp You must be joking.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 你一定是在开玩笑吧。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp This house must belong to John.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这栋房子一定是约翰的。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She must have been young when she got married.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她结婚时一定很年轻。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp You must win, if you do your best.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 如果你全力以赴, 一定能赢。</font><br>(表示坚持)<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp If you must smoke, at least you could use an ashtray.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 如果你一定要吸烟, 起码总可以用一个烟灰缸吧。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Why must you always be finding fault with that girl?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 你为何总是要找那个姑娘的错呢?</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>必须做的事, 必不可少的事物<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Warm clothes are a must in the mountains.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 到山区去穿暖和的衣服是必须的。</font><br>\n
my	<h3>my</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>pron.</i></font><br>我的, 属于我的<br>(用于名词或形容词前作为称呼某人的方式)<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp My dear Anne!</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 亲爱的安妮！</font><br>(用于感叹)<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp My god!</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 天哪！</font><br>\n
name	<h3>name</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>名字, 名称<br>名声; 名誉<br>著名的人物, 名人<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp All the big names in the pop music world were at the party.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 流行音乐界的头号人物都参加了聚会。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt.</i></font><br>给…取名<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Have you named the new baby yet?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 你给新婴儿取名了吗?</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp They named him John.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们给他取名为约翰。</font><br>说出…的名字, 提…的名字; 列举<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The child can name all the flowers in the garden.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 那孩子能说出花园里所有的花名。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Can you name the chief rivers of China?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 你能列举出中国的主要河流吗?</font><br>决定; 任命; 提名<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp They named Smith as president.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们提名史密斯担任主席。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The President named him to be Secretary of State.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 总统任命他为国务卿。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The President named him to head the delegation.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 总统指定他率领代表团。</font><br>\n
nation	<h3>nation</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>国家<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Some nations built their hopes for peace on the talks between big nations.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 有些国家把和平的希望建立在大国之间的谈判上。</font><br>民族<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The British nation has not risen up in a generation.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 英国民族并非在一代时期崛起。</font><br>\n
national	<h3>national</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adj.</i></font><br>国家的, 民族的, 全国性的, 国民的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp These matters are vital to the national security.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这些事情对国家安全至关重要。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp It is a national newspaper.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这是一份全国性报纸。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I love the national culture very much.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我非常喜欢民族文化。</font><br>国有的, 国立的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He graduated from a national university.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他毕业于一所国立大学。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>某国国民<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Foreign nationals were asked to leave the country.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 外国侨民被要求离开该国。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp A consul's duty is to help his own nationals.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 领事的职责是帮助自己的同胞。</font><br>\n
near	<h3>near</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adv.</i></font><br>(空间)在近处; 在附近<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp We live quite near.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们就住在附近。</font><br>(时间)临近, 来临<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The summer holidays are drawing near.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 暑假快到了。</font><br>(程度)几乎, 差不多, 将近<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He was near frozen when they found him.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们找到他时, 他差不多冻僵了。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>prep.</i></font><br>(表示位置)靠近, 在…附近<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The small child was afraid to go near the dog.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 那小孩子不敢靠近那条狗。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp We were near him at the table.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们吃饭时坐在他的附近。</font><br>(表示时间)将近, 快到, 临近<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp It's near five o'clock.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 现在将近五点钟。</font><br>(表示程度)接近, 近乎, 濒临<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Most views were fairly near the truth.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 许多观点与真实情况十分相近。</font><br>(表示关系)与…近似; 与…紧密相关<br>(表示过程)到…去从事活动<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He never goes near a public house.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他从来不到酒馆喝酒。</font><br>(表示数目)大约, 接近<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He must be getting near retiring age.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他一定快到退休年龄了。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adj.</i></font><br>近的; 不远的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Can you tell me the nearest way to the station?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 你能告诉我去火车站最近的路吗?</font><br>亲密的; 近亲的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp We are near relatives.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们是近亲。</font><br>近似, 相似<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Very often tragedies or near tragedies occurred.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 悲剧或近乎悲剧的事经常发生。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt. & vi.</i></font><br>接近; 靠近<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Storm clouds neared.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 暴风雨的乌云迫近了。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He must be nearing home by now.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他现在一定已经快到家了。</font><br>\n
need	<h3>need</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt.</i></font><br>需要; 必须<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp These shoes need to be repaired.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这些鞋需要修理。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp These patients need looking after.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这些病人需要照料。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She needs the work done before tomorrow.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她必须在明天以前找人完成这项工作。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>aux.v.</i></font><br>必须<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Need he go yesterday?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 昨天他有去的必要吗?</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>需要, 需求<br>责任, 必要<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp There is no need of your anxiety.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 你的焦虑是不必要的。</font><br>需要的东西<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The hotel staff will supply all your needs.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 饭店工作人员会向你们提供一切需用的东西。</font><br>贫穷; 困窘<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp We are collecting money for families in need.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们正在为有困难的家庭募捐。</font><br>\n
never	<h3>never</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adv.</i></font><br>从不, 永不, 从来没有<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I can never understand why Mary said nothing about her wrongs.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我毫不理解玛丽说她什么也没有做错。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Neighbours are said never to agree.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 据说, 邻居们永远不会同意。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He never intended to use this method.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他从来没想使用这种方法。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Never having seen him before, I did not know what he looked like.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我从来没见过他, 不知道他长得怎样。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I hope never to see him again.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我希望再不要见到他。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Never have I seen such a strange person.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我从来没见过这样的怪人。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp There is never a friend but he remembers the birthday of.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他记得每个朋友的生日。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I have never been abroad, neither[nor] have I ever wished to go.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我从未去过国外, 我也从未想去。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He never behaves honestly, nor wisely.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他的行为既不诚实, 也不聪明。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp You can tell him now, remember better late than never.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 你现在可以告诉他, 要记得“晚做总比不做好”。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Never mind the expense!</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 不用担心费用！</font><br>\n

news	<h3>news</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>新闻; 消息<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The news was announced as official.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这是以官方消息发布的。</font><br>(可当作新闻内容的)人, 物, 事<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Ill news runs space.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 恶事传千里。</font><br>\n
next	<h3>next</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adj.</i></font><br>紧接在后的, 次于的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp We may go out next Sunday, but that depends.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们可能下星期天郊游, 但那要看情况而定。</font><br>贴近的, 紧邻的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He contrasted his son with the boy next door.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他将他的儿子与隔壁的男孩比较。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adv.</i></font><br>接下去; 然后<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp What are you going to do next?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 然后你要干什么?</font><br>居后地, 次于<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp John arrived first and Jane came next.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 约翰先到了, 然后是简。</font><br>\n

not	<h3>not</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adv.</i></font><br>不, 没<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp They're not students.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们不是学生。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I'm going too, ain't I?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我不是也要去吗?</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I asked him not to come.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我请他不要来。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I don't think it will rain.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我想不会下雨的。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Is she ready or not?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她准备好了没有?</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp All he said is not right.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他说的不全对。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Not until last week was the project in full blast.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 工程直到上星期才全部开工。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Not once have the workers of our factory succeeded in inventing new machines, but many times.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们厂的工人们成功地发明新机器已经不止一次了, 而是许多次了。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The desk is not two feet high.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这张书桌不到两英尺高。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He didn't half like it.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他非常不喜欢它。</font><br>\n
nothing	<h3>nothing</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>pron.</i></font><br>没有东西, 没有事情, 没有一点儿<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Nothing in the world is difficult for one who sets his mind into it.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 天下无难事, 只怕有心人。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp There is nothing in this box, it's empty.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这盒子里没有任何东西, 是空的。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I had nothing stronger than orange juice to drink.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我只喝了橙汁, 没喝酒。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp There is nothing wrong with the machine.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这台机器没什么毛病。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I know nothing about the accident.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 对那次事故我什么也不知道。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp There's nothing that you can do to help.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 你帮不上忙。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He is a metre nothing.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他身高一米整。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>无关紧要的人[事]<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She is an interesting person but her husband is a real nothing.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她是个十分有趣的人, 但她的丈夫真就不及她了。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I feel what a nothing I am!</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我感到我是多么渺小啊！</font><br>\n
now	<h3>now</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adv.</i></font><br>现在, 目前<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I had a headache this morning, but I'm all right now.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我今天早上头疼, 但现在好了。</font><br>立刻, 马上<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp You've got to ask him.It's now or never.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 你得去问他, 马上去否则就没机会了。</font><br>其时, 当时<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Now the noise was very loud.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 此时噪音极大。</font><br>(说话者用以继续进行叙述、请求、警告等转换语气)<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Now be quiet for a few moments and listen to this.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 请安静一会儿, 注意听着。</font><br>\n
number	<h3>number</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>数, 数字; 号码<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Three is my lucky number.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 三是我的幸运数字。</font><br>数目, 数量<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp There is nothing over the number we need.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 在我们需要的数目外没有超过。</font><br>一群人, 一帮人<br>一期, 册<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp There is a story about her in the current number.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 最近一期上有关于她的故事。</font><br>一首乐曲<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She sang several numbers from her latest album.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她唱了几首她近期唱片中的歌曲。</font><br>喜爱的物品; 衣物<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She was wearing a snappy little red number.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她身着一款时髦的红色衣服。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt.</i></font><br>数; 算<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Let's number them from 1 to 20 row by row.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 让我们每行从1数到20。</font><br>给…编号<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp They forgot to number the pages.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们忘了编页码。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>link v.</i></font><br>总共<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The students of our department numbered in the hundreds.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们系的学生总共有几百人。</font><br>\n
of	<h3>of</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>prep.</i></font><br>(表示时间)在…的, 在…之前; 在…期间<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He was born at the turn of the century.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他出生于世纪之交。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp What do you do of a Saturday?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 星期六你干什么?</font><br>(表示方式)根据<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She did it of her own will.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她是自愿这么做的。</font><br>(表示对象)对于, 就…而言<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He felt quite certain of success.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他对成功很有把握。</font><br>(表示原因)由于, 因为<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I was sick of their fun and games.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们的嬉闹让我厌烦。</font><br>(表示方位)在; 位于<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp New York is east of Washington.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 纽约在华盛顿以东。</font><br>(表示范围)在…之中<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Tom is the eldest of the family.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 汤姆是家里年龄最大的。</font><br>(表示结果)在…方面<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The place is easy of access.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这地方容易进入。</font><br>(表示目的)用于…的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp This is a house of prayer.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这是一座教堂。</font><br>(表示否定)缺乏, 没有<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp They were destitute of necessaries of life.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们缺少生活必需品。</font><br>\n
off	<h3>off</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>prep.</i></font><br>(表示位置)在…的外面, 在…的沿海<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The boat anchored off the fort.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 那艘船停在堡垒外面。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The ship sank off the south coast of the island.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 那艘船在岛的南岸沿海沉没。</font><br>(表示时间)在…之前<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp It is a few minutes off three o'clock.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 还有几分钟就三点了。</font><br>(表示方向)从…, 通向, 偏离, 从…离开<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He fell off the ladder.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他从梯子上掉下来。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The kitchen's off the dining room.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 厨房通向餐厅。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp We are going off the subject.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们正偏离正题。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He was off his seat.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他离开他的位子。</font><br>(表示比较)低于, 不及<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp They are selling the bikes off the market price.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们按低于市价卖出自行车。</font><br>(表示否定)不想, 不做<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He is off tea.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他不想喝茶。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She's off work with a bad color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他借我一英镑。</font><br>(表示依附)依靠<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp This bear feeds off the leaves of the tree.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这只熊依靠这棵树的树叶生存。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adv.</i></font><br>离开<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp They drove off.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们开车离开了。</font><br>脱落<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He's had his beard shaved off.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他把胡子剃掉了。</font><br>断开<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The radio is off.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 录音机是关着的。</font><br>光, 完<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp His money was off yesterday.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 昨天他的钱用完了。</font><br>休息<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp We are off one day.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们休息一天。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adj.</i></font><br>休息的; 闲散的; 安静的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The winter is an off offer	<h3>offer</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt.</i></font><br>主动提供; 主动提出; 出价<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The museum offers extensive facilities for study.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这个博物馆提供了许多供研究的设备。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She offered to help me to learn English.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她提出要帮我学英语。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He offered me some tickets.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他给了我几张票。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He offered himself as a candidate.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他自告奋勇要当候选人。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt. & vi.</i></font><br>表示愿意等<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I don't need any help, but it was kind of you to offer.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我不需要任何帮助, 但是你愿意提供帮助, 我很感激。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp They offered to go where there were difficulties.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们表示愿意到艰苦的地方去。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vi.</i></font><br>出现, 显现<br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>提议, 提供<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp If he makes you a good offer, don't refuse it.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 如果他向你提出一个好建议, 你不要拒绝。</font><br>供应; 报价<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I am open to an offer.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我愿考虑买主的出价。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Your offer is a bit too high.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 你出的价太高了。</font><br>\n

oil	<h3>oil</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>油<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Oil and water do not mix.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 油和水不能溶合。</font><br>石油<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Revenues from oil are the biggest single component part in the country's income.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 来自石油的收益是这个国家收入中最高的一项。</font><br>油画; 油画颜料<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp This oil painting is very valuable.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这幅油画很有价值。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt.</i></font><br>给…加油<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp You must oil the tractor every day.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 你必须每天给拖拉机加油。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vi.</i></font><br>化成油<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Butter oils when heated.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 奶油加热就化了。</font><br>\n
old	<h3>old</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adj.</i></font><br>老的; 年老的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He gets tax relief because he supports his old mother.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他因赡养年迈的母亲而得以减税。</font><br>古老的; 古代的, 陈旧的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp It's just an old rag I had in the closet.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这只不过是我挂在壁橱里的旧衣服罢了。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He posed as an expert on old coins.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他假装是个古钱币专家。</font><br>…年龄的; …岁的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp This pine is a hundred years old.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这棵松树的年龄是100岁。</font><br>早已认识的; 熟悉的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I met with an old friend at a dinner party.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我在一次宴会上偶然遇到一位老朋友。</font><br>以前的; 从前的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She got her old job back.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她恢复了过去的工作。</font><br>有经验的, 老练的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp That child seems old beyond his years.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 那个孩子看上去比他的实际年龄老成。</font><br>\n
on	<h3>on</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>prep.</i></font><br>(表示位置)在…上, 在…旁, 在…身边<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp That book on the desk is an atlas.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 事情发生在15号的上午。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp On arriving home, I was met by my daughter.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 到家时我的女儿出来迎接我。</font><br>(表示方向)向, 往, 朝; 沿着, 顺着<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp They marched on the enemy's fortress.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们向敌人的要塞进军。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp We were driving on a California freeway.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们正沿着加利福尼亚的一条快车道驾车行驶。</font><br>(表示状态)系于, 悬于; 附于<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp A picture hangs on the wall.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 墙上挂着一幅画。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He carried a coat on his arm.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他手臂上搭着一件外衣。</font><br>(表示方式)乘, 坐, 骑<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She will leave on an early train.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她将乘早班火车离开。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp We went to the factory on foot.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们步行到工厂去。</font><br>(表示对象)对, 对于, 碰在, 对…造成困难<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp There is much to be said on both sides.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 公说公有理, 婆说婆有理。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The car broke down on us.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 汽车抛锚给我们造成了麻烦。</font><br>(表示原因)由于, 因为<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The old worker retired on account of age.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 老工人因年老而退休。</font><br>(表示比较)与…相比<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Today's weather is an improvement on yesterday's.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 今天的天气比昨天的好。</font><br>(表示方位)在…方位<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The town stands on the left bank of the river.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 该镇坐落在河的左岸。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The post office is on the right.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 邮局在右边。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adv.</i></font><br>(放, 穿, 连接)上<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He has new shoes on.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他穿上新鞋。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She put the tablecloth on.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她铺上了台布。</font><br>向前, (继续)下去<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She worked on quietly all night.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她整个晚上默默地继续工作。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp They walked on a little way without speaking.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们默默无语地向前走了一段路。</font><br>\n
once	<h3>once</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adv.</i></font><br>一次<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I have been there once.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我到过那儿一次。</font><br>曾经, 昔时<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I once went around the world.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 过去我周游过全球。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>conj.</i></font><br>一旦…就…<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Once you begin, you must continue.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 一旦开了头, 你就应当继续下去。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>〈口〉一次, 一回<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She's only done it the once, so don't be too angry.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她只做过这一次, 不要太生气。</font><br>\n
one	<h3>one</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>num.</i></font><br>(数字)一<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp A person has one head and one neck.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 人有一个头和一条脖子。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Please turn to Chapter One.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 请翻到第一章。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>一个人, 任何人, 人们<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp One can't be too careful in matters like this.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 在这种问题上再怎么小心都不为过。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He was very young, not more than twenty-three or four, as indeed one could see at a glance.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他非常年轻, 不会超过23、24岁, 任何人一眼就会看出来。</font><br>(表示与别的对照)某一例[类]<br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>pron.</i></font><br>用于代替表示单个的事或人的名词或名词短语<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp There are only hard chocolates left, we've eaten all the soft ones.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 只剩下巧克力硬糖, 我们把软糖全吃光了。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp My house is the first one on the left.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我的房子是左边第一家。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adj.</i></font><br>某一个<br>某一<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I met her one afternoon in June.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 六月的一天下午我遇到了她。</font><br>同一个<br>惟一的<br>\n
only	<h3>only</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adj.</i></font><br>惟一的, 仅有的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The only French city she enjoyed was Paris.</font></i><br><font 当时就只有他们两人。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Practice is the only way to learn a language well.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 学好一门语言的惟一途径就是实践。</font><br>最好的, 独一无二的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She's the only woman for the job.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她是最适合做这一工作的人。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Only children are sometimes spoilt.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 独生子女有时被宠坏了。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adv.</i></font><br>只有, 才<br><i><font reached the company out of breath only to be told they were fired.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们上气不接下气地赶到公司, 不料却被告知他们被开除了。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I rushed to the door, only to discover that it was locked and barred.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我冲到门边, 却发现门已被锁死了。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Sap passes right through the aphides' bodies, only getting a little thicker and sweeter.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 汁液直接流过蚜虫的身体, 结果只是变得更稠、更甜。</font><br><i><font open	<h3>open</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adj.</i></font><br>开着的; 开放的, 公开的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The outer door was wide open but the inner one was locked.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 外面的门大开着而里面的门锁着。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp They decided to declare Paris an open city.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们决定宣布巴黎为不设防城市。</font><br>空旷的; 开阔的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp An open sea appeared before us.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们前面呈现出广阔的大海。</font><br>坦率的, 无偏见的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She is a very friendly, open person.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她是个非常友好、坦率的人。</font><br>开始营业的; 活动的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The bank isn't open yet.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 那家银行还没有开门营业。</font><br>(职位等)空缺的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Is the teaching vacancy still open?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 教员职位还有空缺吗?</font><br>尚未决定的, 悬而未决的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp This is an open question at the moment.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 此刻这还是个悬而未决的问题。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt. & vi.</i></font><br>(打)开<br>开始; 开设<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The meeting will open the day after tomorrow.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这个会议将于后天开幕。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The chairman opened the Parliament.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 主席宣布议会开始。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Negotiations would probably be opened again.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 谈判可能又要开始。</font><br>\n

other	<h3>other</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adj.</i></font><br>别的, 其他的, 另外的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Are there any other problems?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 还有其他的问题吗?</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Moral beauty ought to be ranked above all other beauty.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 品德之美应列于其他美之上。</font><br>(两个中的)另一个<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp There must be some other reason for him refusing to help.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他不肯帮忙, 一定另有原因。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Every member must bring one other person.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 每个会员必须带一个人来。</font><br>其余的, 剩下的(人或物)<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The other students in my class work in Jinan.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我班其余的同学都在济南工作。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She is older than me but my other sisters are younger.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她比我大, 其余都是我妹妹。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>pron.</i></font><br>其他的, 别的, 另外的人[事物]<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Some people came by car, others came on foot.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 有些人是坐汽车来的, 其他的是走着来的。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I don't like this dress.Show me some others.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我不喜欢这件衣服, 请另外拿几件给我看看。</font><br>其余的人[事物]<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I went swimming while the others played basketball.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我去游泳, 其余的人都去打篮球了。</font><br>\n

outside	<h3>outside</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adv.</i></font><br>在外面, 向外面<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp It's quite dark outside, there's no moon.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 外面很黑, 没有月亮。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Wilson was waiting for him outside.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 威尔逊在外面等他。</font><br>在户外; 露天<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Please let us in, it's cold outside.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 请让我们进去吧, 外面很冷。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>外面, 外部<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The door was locked on the outside.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 那扇门从外面锁上了。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp One should not judge a thing by the outside.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 不能从外表来判断事物。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He was annoyed with complaints made from outside.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他因外界的种种怨言而感到烦恼。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adj.</i></font><br>外部的, 在外面的, 对着外面的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp All the outside doors have locks.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 所有外面的门都上了锁。</font><br>不在主建筑物内的; 外面的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Work went on as usual inside, uninterrupted by outside repairs.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 外部装修, 内部照常营业。</font><br>集团外的, 组织外的, 外界的, 局外的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp They needed the outside help.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们需要来自外界的帮助。</font><br>(选择余地、可能性等)非常小<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp There's just an outside chance we'll get the contract after all.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 说到底, 我们得到那份合同的希望极其渺茫。</font><br>可能性最大的, 最可能的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 150 is an outside estimate.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 150是最高的估计。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>prep.</i></font><br>(表示位置)在[向]…的外面<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp They stood outside the door.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们站在门外。</font><br>(表示范围)超出…的范围<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp You'll have to do it outside office hours.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 你得在上班以外的时间做这件事。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The matter is outside my area of the responsibility.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 此事超出我的责任范围。</font><br>(表示排斥)除了(某人)<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Outside Tom she has no real friends.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她除了汤姆之外没有真正的朋友。</font><br>\n
over	<h3>over</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>prep.</i></font><br>(表示位置)在…的正上方; 在…的上面; 在…的上空<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp There is a lamp over the table.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 桌子正上方有一盏灯。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The clouds are right over us.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 现在云正在我们的头顶上。</font><br>(表示位置)遍布在…上面, 扩展到…全部<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp A smile came over her face.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她的脸上露出了笑容。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Brilliant light poured over me.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 耀眼的光洒遍我的全身。</font><br>(表示方向)越过, 从一边至…的另一边<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Instead of opening the gate, we climbed over it.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们没有开门, 而是从门顶上爬过去的。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp We moved through fields and over ditches.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们穿过田野, 跨过沟渠。</font><br>(表示方向)从…的边缘向下<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The weight of the net pulled him over the edge and into the sea.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 沉重的鱼网把他拖下崖边坠入海中。</font><br>(表示等级或数目)高于; 在…之上, 超过<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I am not in charge of the department; I have two people over me.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我不是这个部门的主管, 我还有两位上级。</font><br>(表示时间或过程)在…期间; 在从事…的时候<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Will you be at home over Christmas?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 你圣诞节期间在家吗?</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The leaders met over informal lunches.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 领袖们在非正式午餐时进行会晤。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp They discussed it over a game of golf.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们一边打高尔夫球, 一边讨论。</font><br>(表示论及)关于, 在…方面<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp These men have quarreled over the price of a load of hay.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这帮人为了一车干草的价钱争吵不休。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adv.</i></font><br>(倒)下, (掉)下, 翻过来<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She knocked the vase over.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她碰倒了花瓶。</font><br>从一边至另一边, 从一方至另一方<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Let's change these two pictures over.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们把两张画对调一下位置。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp We rowed over to the other side of the river.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们划船到河的对岸。</font><br>全部地, 从头至尾<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I have read the paper over.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我把报纸全部看完了。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I have looked all over for him.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我到处都找过他了。</font><br>再一次, 重复地<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp My sums were wrong and I had to do them over.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我的总数错了, 只好再算一遍。</font><br>过分地; 太<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She is over polite.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她太客气了。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He was over nervous.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他太紧张了。</font><br>结束, 了结<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The war was all over.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 战争结束了。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp His suffering will soon be over.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他的苦难就要结束了。</font><br>\n
own	<h3>own</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adj.</i></font><br>属于自己的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Bananas have their own characteristic smell.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 香蕉有其特有的香味。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp My time isn't my own.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我的时间不属于我自己。</font><br>自己做的, 为自己的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She makes all her own clothes.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她的衣服都是自己做的。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp It was my mother's very own engagement ring.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这正是我母亲自己的订婚戒指。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt.</i></font><br>拥有<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Who owns this house?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这房子归谁所有?</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Julie's father owned a business that dealt in bulk orders.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 朱莉的父亲拥有自己的公司, 专门从事大宗订货。</font><br>承认<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The man refused to own the child.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 那人拒绝承认自己是小孩的父亲。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I own that you are right.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我承认你是对的。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He owned himself to be guilty.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他承认自己有罪。</font><br>\n
page	<h3>page</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>页; 张<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The first page of the book is shown on the screen.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 屏幕上映出了这本书的第一页。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I make several pages of notes on his talk.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我对他的谈话做了几页笔记。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp It was originally published in the pages of a magazine.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这篇文章原先发表在一本杂志上。</font><br>〈文〉重要事件<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp These years will be remembered as some of the finest pages in our country's history.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 人民会把这些年看成是我国历史上最美好的几页。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt.</i></font><br>标记…的页数; 翻页<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He paged the book without interest.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他毫无兴趣地标书页。</font><br>喊出名字以寻找<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He paged his wife.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他喊叫着妻子的名字。</font><br>\n
paper	<h3>paper</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>纸, 墙纸<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The public are requested not to throw waste paper in the park.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 公众被要求不得在公园里乱扔废纸。</font><br>〈口〉报纸<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The papers forecast clear skies tomorrow.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 报纸预报明天晴天。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I asked him to fetch me the evening paper.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我请他去给我把晚报拿来。</font><br>文件<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Assemble your papers and put them in the file.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 把你的文件归拢放在这个文件夹内。</font><br>文章, 论文<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp My paper consists of ten pages.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我的论文共10页。</font><br>试卷<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The geography paper was difficult.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 地理试题很难。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The teacher demands that students should turn in their test papers within two hours.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 老师要求学生两小时内交卷。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt. & vi.</i></font><br>贴纸<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp When did your father last time paper the room?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 上次, 你父亲是什么时候用纸裱糊房间的?</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp We're papering the room.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们正在给这间屋子贴壁纸。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt.</i></font><br>用纸覆盖<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She papered the oranges carefully.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她很仔细地用纸把橘子包起来。</font><br>隐瞒; 掩饰<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He agreed to paper over the cracks for the period of the election.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他同意在选举期间暂时把分歧掩盖起来。</font><br>\n
parent	<h3>parent</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>父亲, 母亲; 家长<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp As an only child he was the idol of his parents.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 作为独子, 他是父母的宠儿。</font><br>\n
party	<h3>party</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>社交聚会<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The party was fresh in her memory.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 那次聚会在她脑海中记忆犹新。</font><br>党, 政党<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The party split up into small groups.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 该党分裂为若干小派系。</font><br>一方, 当事人<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The parties to the dispute should be more polite to each other.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 争执双方应相互礼貌些。</font><br>\n
past	<h3>past</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adj.</i></font><br>以前的, 过去的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp These things happened in the past years.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这些事情都发生在过去的年代里。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Winter is past.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 冬天已经过去了。</font><br>结束了的; 不复存在的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp His prime is past.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他的青春已经不复存在了。</font><br>前任的; 已卸任的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He is the past vice-president.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他就是前任副总裁。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>过去, 昔时; 往事<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The past is past.Let us look ahead.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 过去的事已成过去, 让我们向前看吧。</font><br>过去的生活[经历]<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp We know something of his past.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们对他的经历略知一二。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>prep.</i></font><br>(表示时间)迟于, 在…之后, 晚于<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Dancing was kept up till past two.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 舞会一直开到两点以后。</font><br>(表示距离)远于, 在…的更远处<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The hospital is about a mile past the school.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 医院在离学校一英里以外的地方。</font><br>(表示关涉)从…旁边过去, 通过<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp They went past the department store.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们从百货公司的旁边经过。</font><br>(表示程度)超出, 超越<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp It is past my ability.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这是我力所不及的。</font><br>(表示数目)超过, 过于<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The child can't count past 20.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这孩子不能数过20。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adv.</i></font><br>经过, 过<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp A car ran past at full speed.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 一辆汽车以全速驶过。</font><br>\n
pay	<h3>pay</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt. & vi.</i></font><br>付给; 付款<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp This job pays well.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这份工作报酬不错。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp They had to pay rather heavily.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们得付出沉重的代价。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I have paid the milkman this month.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我这个月付款给送奶人了。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He ought to pay the rent.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他应该付房租。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp We refused to pay them their wages.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们拒绝付给他们工资。</font><br>有利可图; (对…)有利, (对…)值得<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Crime doesn't pay.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 犯罪得不偿失。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp It pays to advertise.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 登广告很有用。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt.</i></font><br>给予<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The manager paid her a compliment on her work.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 经理赞扬了她的工作。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>工资<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp His pay goes up every year.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他的工资每年都有增加。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The trade unions bargained away their rights in exchange for a small pay rise.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 工会不惜牺牲自己的权利以换取微薄的加薪。</font><br>\n
peace	<h3>peace</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>和平, 和平时期<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The people desire peace, security and happiness.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 人民向往和平、安全与幸福。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp After a brief peace, war broke out again.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 在短暂的和平之后, 战争又爆发了。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She had a silver peace symbol hanging on a chain around her neck.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她有一个银制的和平标志挂在项链上。</font><br>治安, 社会安定<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp They were charged with disturbing public peace.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们被指控扰乱社会治安。</font><br>安心; 平静<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Knowing that she had arrived safely restored my peace of mind.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 得知她平安到达, 我就安心了。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp All I want is a bit of peace and quiet.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我所希望的只是一点平静。</font><br>\n
people	<h3>people</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>人, 人们; 一般的人<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The doorman allowed the people in one by one.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 看门的让人们一个一个进去。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Were there many people at the meeting?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 参加会议的人多吗?</font><br>人民; 平民; 老百姓<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The wisdom of the people is inexhaustible.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 人民的智慧是无穷无尽的。</font><br>种族, 民族<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The Japanese are an industrious people.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 日本人民是勤劳的民族。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The peoples of Southeast Asian countries all denounced the treaty between these two countries.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 东南亚各族人民一致声讨这两个国家签订的条约。</font><br>家人, 亲属<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp My husband's people are staying with us now.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我丈夫家里的人现在在我们这儿。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt.</i></font><br>居住于; 使…充满<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp His race has peopled this island through all recorded history.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 自有历史记载以来, 他的族人都居于此岛。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The meadow is peopled with wild flowers.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 草地长满了野花。</font><br>\n
per	<h3>per</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>prep.</i></font><br>〈拉〉(表示关涉)通过, 由<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Do you send the goods per rail, or per plane?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 你送这个商品是通过铁路还是飞机?</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Your car, per Mary, has reached me.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 你的车由玛丽给我。</font><br>(表示根据)依照, 根据<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp You bought goods per list price.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 你按照所列价格买商品。</font><br>(表示比率)(尤指数量, 价格, 时间)每<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp These apples cost 40 pence per pound.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这些苹果每磅40便士。</font><br>\n
perhaps	<h3>perhaps</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adv.</i></font><br>或许, 大概, 可能<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp If you are good I shall perhaps take you for a walk this afternoon.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 如果你乖, 我今天下午可能带你出去散散步。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I perhaps come across him tomorrow.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我明天也许会偶然遇到他。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp You want to make stay long in Beijing, perhaps?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 你要在北京呆很长一段时间吗?</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Perhaps I am wrong, but I think she is over 60 years old.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我也许记错了, 不过我想她已60出头了。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Perhaps it will rain in the afternoon.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 下午可能有雨。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Perhaps they are in need of our help.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 或许他们需要我们的帮助。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Perhaps I can help you.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 也许我能帮帮你的忙吧。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Perhaps this is his finest novel yet.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这也许是至今为止他写得最好的一部小说。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Perhaps you would be good enough to explain this for me.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 请您为我解释这个, 行吗?</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Perhaps you would be kind enough to read this.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 就请你把它念一念好吗?</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Perhaps you would like to see it?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 你可能想看这东西吧?</font><br>\n

剧本<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The college drama society is going to put on a play.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 大学戏剧协会正准备上演一个剧目。</font><br>自由活动<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp We need more play on the rope.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 绳子要松些。</font><br>赌博<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He won 1000 pounds in last night's play.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他昨天晚上赌博赢了1000英镑。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt. & vi.</i></font><br>玩, 玩耍<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Let's go out and play.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们出去玩吧。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He played truant.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他逃学。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The children don't know how to play the game.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 孩子们不会玩这个游戏。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I'll play you a game of cards.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我和你打一场牌。</font><br>参加比赛<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Our best defender is injured and won't be able to play today.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们最佳的防守员受伤了, 今天不能参加比赛。</font><br>演奏; 播放<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The band is playing.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 乐队正在演奏。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He plays the piano surprisingly well.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他钢琴弹得好极了。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Play us something happy.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 为我们演奏一些快乐的乐曲。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He'd written a tune, and played it to us on the piano.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他写了一段曲子, 并在钢琴上弹给我们听。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He played his favourite record for me.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他为我放他最喜爱的唱片。</font><br>演出, 扮演<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The second actor plays well.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 第二个演员演得好。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The dog played dead.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这狗装死。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt.</i></font><br>开某人玩笑, 嘲弄<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Don't play jokes on the poor girl.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 别再开这可怜的女孩玩笑了。</font><br>\n

point	<h3>point</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>要点, 论点, 观点<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Some of these points will have to be further elaborated as we go along.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这些要点中, 有些我们在往下讨论时还得作进一步的详细阐述。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp His remarks lack point.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他的言词缺乏要点。</font><br>尖端; 尖儿<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp When you buy new pens, get one with a sharper point.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 买新钢笔时要买尖儿比较尖的。</font><br>点; 小数点<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp When we read out 4.23, we say “four point two three”.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们把4.23读作四点二三。</font><br>(某一)时刻; (某一)地点<br>分数, 得分<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He conceded ten points to his opponent.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他让给自己的对手十分。</font><br>目的, 意图<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp If you have a definite purpose in mind, get to the point promptly.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 如果你心里有明确的意图, 就干脆说出来。</font><br>条款; 细目<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp There is another point to be borne in mind.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 另外一项条款是应当记住的。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt.</i></font><br>削尖<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Point this pencil for me, please.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 请把铅笔给我削尖。</font><br>增强<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He told a story to point his advice.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他讲了一个故事, 以增强他的忠告的力量。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt. & vi.</i></font><br>指; 指向<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp It's rude to point.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 用手指人是不礼貌的。</font><br>\n

quick	<h3>quick</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adj.</i></font><br>快的, 迅速的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp They took a quick train.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们乘坐快车。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Who will be there quickest?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 谁将最快到那里?</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He is quick at calculation.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他计算的速度很快。</font><br>短时间做成的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp After a quick courtship they married.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们经过一番短暂的恋爱就结婚了。</font><br>易受激发的; 敏感的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She is quick at taking offence.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她容易生气。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He is quick to take offence.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他容易发怒。</font><br>灵活的, 灵敏的; 伶俐的, 机警的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Nothing can escape her quick ear.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 没有什么能逃过她灵敏的耳朵。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Her quick wits saved the boy's life.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她靠机智救了那男孩一命。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He is quick of perception.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他感觉灵敏。</font><br>聪明的, 有能力的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp My son is a quick student and always has high grade.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我儿子是个聪明的学生, 总是得高分。</font><br>\n
quite	<h3>quite</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adv.</i></font><br>完全地; 整体地; 十分地<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Are you quite ready?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 你完全准备好了吗?</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The news is quite amazing.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这消息十分惊人。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I quite like some rock music.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我很喜欢某些摇滚乐。</font><br>有几分; 颇; 相当<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp It was quite good, but not perfect.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 它相当不错, 但还不完善。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He is a quite skilled worker.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他是个相当熟练的工人。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Our meeting in London was quite by chance.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们在伦敦的会面颇为偶然。</font><br>〈尤英〉同意, 不错; 对的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He is quite drunk.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他确实喝醉了。</font><br>\n
race	<h3>race</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>人种, 种族<br>(速度)比赛, 赛跑; 竞争<br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt. & vi.</i></font><br>和…比速度; (使)参加比赛<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He's a very good swimmer and often races.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他是个优秀游泳选手, 经常参加比赛。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Are you going to race your horse at Newmarket next week?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 你要让你的马参加下周在纽马克特的赛马会吗?</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp My horse has hurt his toe so I can't race him.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我的马伤了脚趾, 我不能骑它比赛。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Some medieval towns raced donkeys or buffaloes.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 有些中世纪的城市用驴子或水牛竞赛。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I'll race you home.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我和你比赛看谁先到家。</font><br>(使)快速移动<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The children raced towards me.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 孩子们飞快地向我跑来。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He raced his car across the desert.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他开车驶过那片荒漠。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Let's race to see what is happening.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 咱们跑去看看发生了什么事情。</font><br>\n

无线电接收机突然停了。</font><br>无线电广播台<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The radio broadcast the news in detail.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 无线电台详细地广播了那则消息。</font><br>无线电, 无线电传送, 无线电广播<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp We contacted with the ship by radio.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们通过无线电与那只船取得了联系。</font><br><font 他们利用无线电向伦敦请示。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The ship radioed a call for help.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 那艘船用无线电发出求救信号。</font><br><i><font headquarters that we were in trouble.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们向总部报告, 说我们遇到了困难。</font><br>\n
raise	<h3>raise</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt.</i></font><br>提起; 举起; 竖起<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp When he saw the principal, he raised his hand in salutation.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他看到校长时举手敬礼。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I'll raise both hands in favour of damming the river.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我举双手赞成拦河筑坝。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp From then on we raised our heads and became our own masters.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 从此我们抬起头来当家做主了。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Slowly he raised his bow and began to take aim at the bird.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 慢慢地他举起弓, 开始瞄准那只鸟。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Raise the overturned lamp.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 扶起倒了的灯。</font><br>增加; 提升<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp They raised their output by more than half in less than three years.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 不到三年, 他们把产量提高了一半还多。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp We must do everything we can to raise the people's living standards.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们要想一切办法来提高人民的生活水平。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp None of them raised any objection.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们谁也没提出反对意见。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Why didn't you raise the question at the meeting?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这问题你怎么没有在会上提出来?</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp As no one raised his voice against the plan, it was agreed on.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 由于没有人提反对意见, 那项计划便通过了。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp They decided to raise money by subscription.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们决定靠募捐的办法来筹集这笔款子。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp How were they going to raise enough money for it?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们怎样来为此筹集足够的资金呢?</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp They increased their income by raising silkworms and so on.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们靠养蚕等增加了收入。</font><br>抚养; 饲养<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The old man likes raising rabbits, chickens, dogs and horses.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这个老人喜欢养兔子、鸡、狗和马。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp They raised five thousand chrysanthemums last year.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 去年他们种了五千株菊花。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp We want to raise our children to be decent men and women.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们盼望把孩子们培养成优秀人才。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>(工资、薪金的)提升, 增加<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He went to ask for a raise.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他要求增加工资。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The workers went on strike for a raise.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 工人举行罢工, 要求增加工资。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The trade unions bargained away their rights in exchange for a small pay raise.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 工会不惜牺牲自己的权利以换取微薄的加薪。</font><br>\n
rate	<h3>rate</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>比率, 率<br>(运动、变化等的)速度; 进度<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp We drove at a steady rate.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们以平稳的速度开车。</font><br>费用, 价格<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp We have to offer higher rates.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们不得不付更高的价钱。</font><br>房地产税, 市政服务税<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The rates have gone up.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 房地产税已经提高了。</font><br>等级, 水准<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp This is a first-rate restaurant.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这是一级饭店。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt.</i></font><br>估价; 评估征税现值<br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt. & vi.</i></font><br>认为; 把…算作<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Hong Kong rates as the biggest trade centre in Asia.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 香港被认为是亚洲最大的贸易中心。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp How do you rate our team's chances of winning?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 你认为我们队获胜的概率是多少?</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I would rate this wine as the finest I have ever tasted.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我认为这种酒是我所品尝过的最好的酒。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt., link v.</i></font><br>定级<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Her performance didn't rate high in the competition.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她的表演在这次比赛中等级不算高。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp They rated the new film.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们给那部新片定了级。</font><br>\n
