strong	<h3>strong</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adj.</i></font><br>强壮的, 强有力的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He is as strong as oxen.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他健壮得如牛一样。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The firm ran up against strong competition.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这家公司遇到了强有力的竞争。</font><br>牢固的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He wore strong shoes.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他穿着结实的鞋。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The hedge of stones is much stronger than a wood hedge.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 石头围墙比竹篱笆结实多了。</font><br>坚强的; 坚定的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She has a very strong will.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她有着坚强的意志。</font><br>强烈的, 浓烈的, 深刻的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He has a strong desire to meet you.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他极想见你。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I'm strong against the proposal.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我坚决反对这项建议。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp It's a bit strong to punish her for such a small thing.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 为那么点小事就惩罚她未免有些过分了。</font><br>擅长于…的; 对…很热心的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Making speeches is one of his strong points.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 演讲是他的强项之一。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He is strong in English.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他精通英语。</font><br>\n

such	<h3>such</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adj.</i></font><br>这样的; 如此的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He spent all his money, he is such a fool.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他这样傻, 花光了所有的钱。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Everyone was indoors on such a night.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 在这样的晚上谁都会待在室内。</font><br>这么大的; 非常的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He's such a kind man.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他十分和蔼可亲。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The garage did such a bad repair.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 修车厂的活干得如此之差。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>pron.</i></font><br>这样的事物[人]<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He claimed to be a scholar but was not such.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他自称是个学者, 但实际上并非如此。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Such is life!</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 人生就是这样。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Such are the most powerful voices of our times!</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这些就是我们时代的最有力的声音！</font><br>\n

赞成; 供养<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Our school is supported by the government.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 政府赞助我校的办学费用。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She supports birth control.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她赞成计划生育。</font><br>经常光顾; 为…捧场<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Which football team do you support?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 你支持哪个足球队?</font><br>忍受<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I can't support this heat.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我忍受不了这样的热度。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>支撑, 承受, 支持, 赞助<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Your support has meant a lot to me during this difficult time.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 在这困难时期, 你的支持给了我很大的帮助。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The plan was canceled because of lack of support.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 由于缺乏赞助, 这项计划被取消了。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The argument lacked support.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这一论点缺乏证据。</font><br>支撑物, 支柱, 支座, 支架<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Put a support under it.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 在它下面放一根支柱。</font><br>给予帮助[同情]的人<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Jimmy was a great support to us when father died.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 父亲死后, 吉米给我们的帮助是巨大的。</font><br>支持者, 拥护者<br>\n

this	<h3>this</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adj.</i></font><br>(指已知的或即将提到的人、事物、主意)这, 这个, 此, 本<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Mosquitoes are extremely abundant in this dark wet place.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这个阴暗潮湿的地方蚊子非常多。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp This book of Joe's is very amusing.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 乔的这本书非常有趣。</font><br>(时间、地点、思想等)较近的一个, 这一个<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp They have built three nuclear power stations this year.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们今年建造了三座核电站。</font><br>〈非正〉某个<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp This little daughter of his is very clever.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他的这个小女儿真聪明。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>pron.</i></font><br>这个, 这事<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp This is the man you are going to see, isn't it?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这就是你要见的那个人, 对吗?</font><br>这<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I am one with you on this.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 在这一点上, 我和你的意见是一致的。</font><br>这时; 这里<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I thought he'd have got back before this.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我以为他会在这之前回来的。</font><br>\n

though	<h3>though</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>conj.</i></font><br>虽然; 尽管<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Though he's fool, I like him nonetheless.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 虽然他很笨, 我仍然喜欢他。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp It's quite pleasant today, though the wind is rather cool.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 尽管风有点凉, 今天天气还是很不错的。</font><br>然而; 但是<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She'll probably disagree, though it's worth trying.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她很可能不同意, 但不妨去试一下。</font><br>\n
thought	<h3>thought</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>思索, 思维能力; 思考的过程<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp After some thought he hit on a plan to route the enemy.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他经过一番思考, 想到了一个打垮敌人的办法。</font><br>思想, 思潮<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp His thought is beyond the reach of my imagination.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他的思想不是我所能想像得到的。</font><br>关心, 注意, 考虑<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The nurse is always full of thought for her patients.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这名护士对病人总是关心备至。</font><br>想法, 观点<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Why do you hide your thoughts from me?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 你为什么对我隐瞒你的想法?</font><br>意向, 意图<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She had no thought of going.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她没有走的意向。</font><br>\n
thousand	<h3>thousand</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>num.</i></font><br>一千<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp There are thousands of people on the square.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 广场上有成千上万的人。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He has collected more than a thousand stamps.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他已收集了一千多张邮票。</font><br>\n
three	<h3>three</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>num.</i></font><br>三<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp They left by twos and threes.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们三三两两地离开。</font><br>\n
through	<h3>through</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>prep.</i></font><br>(表示位置)在…之中; 在…各处; 遍及<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The earth moves through space.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 地球在太空中运行。</font><br>(表示时间)在…期间; 从…开头到结尾<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Tom bore up bravely through his father's illness.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 在他父亲生病期间, 汤姆表现得很坚强勇敢。</font><br>(表示方向)从…的一端到另一端; 经过<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He went through the forest the next day.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 次日他穿过了森林。</font><br>(表示状态)经历着; 度过<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He has decided to prolong his visit through the weekend.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他已决定把他的访问延长到过完周末。</font><br>(表示方式)凭借; 用<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I learnt of the position through a newspaper advertisement.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我是从报纸广告上得悉有此职位的。</font><br>(表示原因)因为, 由于<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp It was through him that I missed my train.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 就是因为他, 我才误了火车。</font><br>(表示让步)尽管有(反对、抗议等)的声音; 顶着<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The politician struggled to speak through the shouts of the crowd.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 尽管人群中不断有叫喊声, 那位政客仍然坚持讲下去。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adv.</i></font><br>通过, 过去<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Can I get through by this road?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我可以从这条路过去吗?</font><br>进行到底<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I'm counting on you to help me through!</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我正指望你帮忙帮到底呢！</font><br>\n
time	<h3>time</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>时间<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The philosopher speculated about time and space.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这位哲学家在思索时间和空间问题。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp What time is it?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 现在几点钟?</font><br>次, 回<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He told the same style old jokes I've heard fifty times before.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他讲的老笑话, 我已听过五十遍了。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp When I saw him the second time, he had already got married.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我第二次见到他时, 他已结婚了。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Three times four is[are] twelve.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 三乘四等于十二。</font><br>时代, 时期<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp It doesn't meet the requirements of the times.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 它不适应时代的要求。</font><br>时机, 做某种活动的时候<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp This time is ripe for action.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 采取行动的时机已经成熟。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp It is high time for action.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 该采取行动了。</font><br>\n
to	<h3>to</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>prep.</i></font><br>(表示时间)到, 直到, 在…到来之前, 离…<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The Parliament was prorogued to the tenth of February.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 议会休会到二月十日。</font><br>(表示方向)朝, 往, 通向<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He turned to his companion before he replied.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他转身朝向他的伙伴然后回答。</font><br>(表示状态)紧贴着, 紧靠着, 对着<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The two lovers danced cheek to cheek.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 那对情侣脸贴着脸跳舞。</font><br>(表示对象)对, 对于, 对…来说<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp What will Doris say to it?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 对此事多丽丝将怎么说呢?</font><br>(表示比较)比, 相对于<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The men are noodles to her.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 与她相比, 这些男人都是笨蛋。</font><br>(表示方位)在…方向[方位], 处于…顺序<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Scotland is to the north of England.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 苏格兰在英格兰之北。</font><br>(表示距离)离, 距离<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp It is ten kilometres to the station.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 到车站十公里。</font><br>(表示目标)到达, 直到<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp We came to a picturesque cottage.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们来到一座风景如画的村落。</font><br>(表示结果)转换为, 转变为, 趋于<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Wait until the lights change to green.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 等交通灯变成绿色再走。</font><br>\n
today	<h3>today</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adv.</i></font><br>(在)今天<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The meeting today is very important.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 今天的会议很重要。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp They are coming here today week.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们将在下星期的今天来这里。</font><br>现在, 现今, 现代<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Full-length coats are vogue today.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 如今流行长外套。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>今天<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Today is Sunday.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 今天是礼拜天。</font><br>现代, 当代<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He is a writer of today.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他是位当代作家。</font><br>\n
together	<h3>together</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adv.</i></font><br>在一起; 共同<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp They often confer together.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们经常在一起协商。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He did more than the rest of us did together.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他做的比我们其余人合在一起做的还要多。</font><br>同时, 一齐<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Don't all speak together.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 不要都同时说话。</font><br>一致地, 协调地<br>不间断地; 连续地<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The man talked for hours together.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这个人一连讲了几个小时。</font><br>\n
too	<h3>too</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adv.</i></font><br>也, 还<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp They are coming tomorrow and I hope you will come too.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们明天要来, 我希望你也来。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Here, too, the colon must be followed by a dash.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这里也是一样, 应当在冒号后加破折号。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Too, the reader will find in this book many interesting illustrations.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 读者还能在书中看到许多有趣的插图。</font><br>太, 过于<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He was evidently too tired to go any further.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他显然太疲劳, 一步也走不动了。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp This box is too heavy to be lifted.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这箱子太重搬不起来。</font><br>很, 非常<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Beginners are too apt to make mistakes in grammar.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 初学者极易犯语法错误。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp We are all too pleased to listen to the opinions of other.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们非常乐意听别人的意见。</font><br>\n
top	<h3>top</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>顶, 顶部<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp When you reach the top of the hill, bear to the right.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 当你到达山顶时, 向右转。</font><br>上部, 上端<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She feared for the little boy when she saw him at the top of the tree.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她看到那个小男孩在树顶上时, 着实替他捏了一把汗。</font><br>首位, 最高位, 精华<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He is at the top of his class.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他是班上最优秀的学生。</font><br>盖<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp That top belongs to this box.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 那个盖子是这个盒子的。</font><br>陀螺<br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adj.</i></font><br>最高的, 最优良的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp There was a fire in the top story of the building.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 大楼的顶层着火了。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She is top in French.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她的法语学得最好。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt.</i></font><br>给…加顶; 给…盖盖子<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He is going to top the barn tomorrow.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他打算明天给粮仓封顶。</font><br>达到…的顶端<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp A church tops the hill.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 山顶有一座教堂。</font><br>超过; 胜过; 高过<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He tops the rest in scholarship.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他的学识超过其他人。</font><br>\n
total	<h3>total</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adj.</i></font><br>总计的; 全部的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Please figure out the total cost.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 请算出总费用。</font><br>完全的; 全然的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp My efforts ended in total failure.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我的努力终归全盘失败。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The destruction was total.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这场毁灭是彻底的。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>总计, 总数<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp A total of twenty people were[was] killed.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 共有二十人被杀。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt. & vi.</i></font><br>计算<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Please total all the expenditures.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 请计算一下全部支出是多少。</font><br>\n
towards	<h3>towards</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>prep.</i></font><br>向, 朝<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He headed towards the station.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他向车站赶去。</font><br>为了<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The United Nations' work is towards peace.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 联合国的工作是为了实现和平。</font><br>对于, 关于<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He is friendly towards me.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他对我友好。</font><br>接近<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp We arrived towards night.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们接近半夜才到达。</font><br>\n
town	<h3>town</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>镇, 市镇<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The town is a residential suburb.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这个小镇是市郊住宅区。</font><br>城镇居民<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The whole town is[are] furious about the council's education policy.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 全镇居民对市政会的教育政策都感到极其愤怒。</font><br>商业中心[闹市区]<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He is going into town this morning.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他上午打算到商业区去。</font><br>\n
trade	<h3>trade</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>贸易, 商业<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Transport has always been the key to developing trade.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 运输一直是发展贸易的关键。</font><br>行业, 生意<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Which is your trade?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 你做哪一行?</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp They carried on trade in tea and spices with the orient.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们同东方国家做茶叶和香料的生意。</font><br>谋生手段, 手艺, 职业<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Shoemaking is a useful trade.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 做鞋是一种有用的手艺。</font><br>同仁, 同行<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Only is the trade likely to be interested in this talk.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 只有同行才可能对这个话题感兴趣。</font><br>〈美〉顾客<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp A lot of trade are in that store.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 那商店有许多顾客。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt. & vi.</i></font><br>交易; 经商<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He traded as a tobacco merchant.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他是做烟草生意的商人。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp They traded seats.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们互换座位。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp They were persuaded to trade information.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们被说服出卖情报。</font><br>\n
try	<h3>try</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt. & vi.</i></font><br>试图; 努力<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp If you can't do it the first time, try again.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 要是你第一次做不成, 就再试一下。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He tried climbing the tall tree.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他试着爬上那棵大树。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He has been trying to solve the problem.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他一直在设法解决这一问题。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Let me try retelling the story.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 让我试着复述这个故事吧。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Try what you can do.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 试试看你能有什么办法。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Try how far you can throw.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 试试看你能扔多远。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Let's try which takes most.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 咱们试试哪种办法费时间最多。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Let's try whether it will break.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 咱们来试试, 看它会不会折断。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She tried herself to vote	<h3>vote</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt.</i></font><br>一致认为<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The students voted to continue the struggle.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 学生们一致决定继续斗争。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp They voted that the meeting should be adjourned.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们一致认为应该休会。</font><br>提议, 建议<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I vote that he (should) do it.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我建议他做那件事。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt. & vi.</i></font><br>投票, 表决<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp You're too young to vote.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 你太小, 不能参加选举。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp They vote to choose a president.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们投票选举总统。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Vote MacDonald, the man you can trust!</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 请投麦克唐纳的票, 他是大家能信任的人！</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp We have voted him our monitor.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们选他当班长。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>投票, 选举, 表决<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The vote will be held next month.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 下个月举行选举。</font><br>票, 选票<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The Tory got 40% of the vote.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 保守党获得40%的选票。</font><br>表决结果; 投票总数<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Was the vote for or against the resolution?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 表决结果是赞成还是反对此决议?</font><br>选举权, 投票权, 表决权<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Only members of the team have a vote.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 只有这个团体的成员才有表决权。</font><br>\n
wait	<h3>wait</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt. & vi.</i></font><br>等候, 等待<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp We shan't wait long.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们不会等很久的。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp That waiter does not know how to wait.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 那侍者不会侍候顾客。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I'm waiting to hear your explanation.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我在等你的解释。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He's waiting his opportunity.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他正等候机会。</font><br>\n
walk	<h3>walk</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt. & vi.</i></font><br>走, 步行, 散步<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The baby can't walk yet.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这婴儿还不会走。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The old man walked five miles every morning.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这老人每天早晨步行五英里。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He walked slow and lame.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他慢慢地一瘸一拐地走着。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The trainer is walking his dogs.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 那位驯兽人正在遛他的狗。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>步行, 散步<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Uncle Tom looked hot after his walk.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 在步行之后, 汤姆叔叔看来很热。</font><br>行走的路程<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp It's a long walk to the station.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 去车站要走很长一段路。</font><br>步态<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He ran, and then slowed down to a walk.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他跑着, 然后放慢速度步行。</font><br>步行的路径<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The walk was covered with leaves.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这人行道上满是树叶。</font><br>\n
wall	<h3>wall</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>墙, 壁, 围墙<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp They glided along the wall until they were out of sight.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们沿着墙壁溜得无影无踪。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He fastened the calendar to a wall.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他把日历挂在墙上。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I should hate to be confined within the four walls of an office all day.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我讨厌整天关在办公室里。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt. & vi.</i></font><br>筑墙围住, 用墙隔开<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp We're going to wall the garden.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们打算用墙把花园围起来。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp They walled off the large prison into lots of very small cells.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们把大监狱隔成很多小牢房。</font><br>\n
want	<h3>want</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt.</i></font><br>打算, 希望<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I want your promise.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我希望你答应。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The picture wants something of perfection.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这幅画还有些不够完美。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I've long wanted to come to your country.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我老早就想到你们国家来。</font><br>应该<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I want a shave.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我该刮胡子了。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Your watch wants repairing.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 你的手表该修一修了。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt. & vi.</i></font><br>想, 要, 需要<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp You shall never want while I have any money left.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 只要我有余钱, 就不会叫你缺少什么。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp These plants are drooping—they want water.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这些庄稼有点枯萎——需要浇水。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>缺乏, 不足<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Your work shows want of care.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 你的工作证明你缺乏细心。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The plants died for want of water.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这些植物因缺水而枯死了。</font><br>需要的东西, 想往的东西<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp You should try to reduce your wants.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 你应该努力减少需求。</font><br>\n
war	<h3>war</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>战争; 战争期间<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp They were fighting a just war.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们在打一场正义战争。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Their courage brought the people through the war.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们的勇气使人们熬过了战争。</font><br>斗争, 竞争<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp They are at war with each other.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们互相争吵。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vi.</i></font><br>进行战斗; 作战<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The two countries have been warring constantly for years.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这两国多年来一直交战。</font><br>斗争<br>\n
water	<h3>water</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>水<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Flowers will die without water.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 没有水, 花就会枯死。</font><br>大片的水, (尤指)湖[河, 海]<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp They forbid any ships to enter the water.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们禁止任何船舶进入这片水域。</font><br>(湖、河等的)水域, (某国附近的)海域<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The ship is in British waters.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这条船行驶在英国的海域里。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt.</i></font><br>在…浇水[洒水]<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Water the flowers every morning.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 每天早晨给花浇水。</font><br>给…水喝<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Have the horses been fed and watered?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 给马匹喂食饮水了吗?</font><br>(尤指江河)流经并供水给(某地区)<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The valley is continuously watered by the melting snow from the mountains.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 群山融化的雪不断流经山谷。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vi.</i></font><br>流眼泪; 流口水<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The smoke made her eyes water.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 烟熏得她眼睛流泪。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The smell from the kitchen made his mouth water.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 从厨房传来的气味使他流口水。</font><br>\n
way	<h3>way</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>路, 道, 街, 径<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Is this the way out?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这是出去的路吗?</font><br>方向<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Kindly step this way, ladies and gentlemen.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 女士们、先生们, 请往这边走。</font><br>方法, 方式, 手段<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp They are trying to find a way of settling the dispute.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们正设法寻找解决争端的办法。</font><br>习俗; 作风; 习惯<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The way that you're doing it is completely crazy.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 你这种习惯, 简直是发疯了。</font><br>距离<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Success is still a long way off.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 离成功还远着呢。</font><br>附近, 周围<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The crops are doing well down this way.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这一带的作物长势良好。</font><br>某方面<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The doctor told the patient that he was in good way.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 大夫对病人说, 他的病情已在好转。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adv.</i></font><br>远远地, 大大地<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The mortality rate was way down.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 死亡率大大降低。</font><br>\n

what	<h3>what</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>pron.</i></font><br>(用以询问某人或某事物的词) 什么, 多少<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp What is the price?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 价钱多少?</font><br>…的事物<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp This dictionary is just what I want for my study.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这部词典正是我学习要用的工具。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adj.</i></font><br>…的(事物或人)<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp What colour is it?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 它是什么颜色的?</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adv.</i></font><br>(用于感叹句中)<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp What genius he has!</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他真有才华！</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp What happy children they are!</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们是些多么幸福的孩子呀！</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>int.</i></font><br>(用以表示不相信或惊奇)<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp What, do you really mean it?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 什么, 你真是这个意思?</font><br>(用以表示未听清楚对方说的话)<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp What?Can you say that again?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 什么?你能再说一遍吗?</font><br>\n
when	<h3>when</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adv.</i></font><br>什么时候<br>在那时, 其时<br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>conj.</i></font><br>在…时, 当时<br>如果, 要是<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp When the weather is good, I usually go to the country.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 若是天气好的话, 我总是到乡下去。</font><br>既然, 考虑到<br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>pron.</i></font><br>什么时候<br>那时<br>\n
where	<h3>where</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adv.</i></font><br>在哪里, 到哪里, 在什么位置<br>在…(地方); 到…(地方)<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp This is the house where the great man was born.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这所房子便是那位伟人出生的地方。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She was shown into a small room, where there was a dying man.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她被领进了一间小屋子, 那里有一个垂死的人。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>conj.</i></font><br>(在)…的地方<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp They live where the police can't get them.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他们住在警察抓不到他们的地方。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp That's where it is.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 那才是真正的理由所在。</font><br>\n
whether	<h3>whether</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>conj.</i></font><br>是否<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She was in doubt whether she was right.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她对她是否正确拿不准。</font><br>不管…(还是…)<br>\n
which	<h3>which</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>pron.</i></font><br>哪一个, 哪一些<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp That is the house which I built.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 那是我建的房子。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Ask him which he wants.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 问他一下他要哪一个。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I can't decide which to choose.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我无法决定要选哪一个。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adj.</i></font><br>哪一<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Let me know which train you'll be arriving on.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 告诉我你要坐哪一趟车来。</font><br>\n
white	<h3>white</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adj.</i></font><br>白色的, 白的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She wore white trousers.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她穿着白色的裤子。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She smiled, showing all her strong white teeth.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她笑了, 露出一口洁白的好牙齿。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp His hair has turned white.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他的头发已经变白了。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp No wool is so white but a dyer can dye it black.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 任何白羊毛都能被染黑。</font><br>白种人的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp In the city there are many black people as well as white people.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 城里除了白人外还有许多黑人。</font><br>脸色苍白的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She went as white as a sheet when she heard the news.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她听到这个消息后脸色苍白。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>白色<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp White and black are opposites.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 白色和黑色是对比颜色。</font><br>白种人<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp There are many whites in our town.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们镇上有很多白人。</font><br>蛋清, 蛋白<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She used the whites of six eggs to make the cake.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她用了六个鸡蛋的蛋白来做蛋糕。</font><br>\n
who	<h3>who</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>pron.</i></font><br>谁, 什么人<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Who is that woman in the red hat?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 那个戴红色帽子的女人是谁?</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I wonder who will play in the basketball match.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我不知道这场篮球赛谁会上场。</font><br>(限制性关系代词)…人<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He who laughs last laughs best.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 最后笑的人笑得最开心。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp All who[that] heard him were delighted.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 所有听了他讲话的人都很高兴。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He is the only one who[that] knows Russian.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他是我们中间惟一懂俄语的人。</font><br>(非限制性关系代词)他, 她, 他们<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The committee, who were all young women, fulfilled their duties admirably.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 委员会的委员们都是些年轻妇女, 很好地履行了她们的职责。</font><br>\n
whole	<h3>whole</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adj.</i></font><br>齐全的, 整体的, 全部的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The whole village was attacked with influenza.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 整个村子的人都得了流行性感冒。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The old woman has been confined to her bed for a whole year.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 那老妇人已经卧病在床整整一年了。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Forty is a whole number.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 40是个整数。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp That's the whole truth about it.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这就是事情的全部真相。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He ate an apple whole.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他把整个苹果一口吃下。</font><br>没有破碎的; 完整的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp You're lucky to escape with a whole skin.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 你未受损伤而逃脱, 真是幸运。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Did you break the whole dish?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 盘子被你打碎了?</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He was surprised to find himself whole after the accident.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他惊奇地发现自己在事故发生后安然无恙。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>齐全, 整体, 全部<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The whole of my money was stolen.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我全部的钱都被偷走了。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He spent the whole of the week in hospital.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他住院住了整整一星期。</font><br>整体, 一体<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Two halves make a whole.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 两个一半构成一个整体。</font><br>\n
whose	<h3>whose</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>pron.</i></font><br>谁的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Whose is this?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这是谁的?</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp These books are mine, then whose are those?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这些书是我的, 那些书是谁的?</font><br>那个[些](人)的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp That's the man whose house was burned down.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这就是房子被大火烧了的那个人。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The men whose names were called left the room.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 那些被叫到名字的人离开了房间。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The play, whose style is rigidly formal, is typical of the period.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这剧本是那个时期的典型作品, 风格拘谨刻板。</font><br>\n
why	<h3>why</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adv.</i></font><br>为什么<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Why are you late?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 你为什么迟到?</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Why not call on me tomorrow?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 你干吗不明天就来看我呢?</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp That is why I'm working hard at my lesson.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 就是这个原因, 我要努力学习。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I can't understand why he failed.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我不明白他为什么失败了。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp That is the reason why we must go now.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 那就是我们现在必须走的理由。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Why ever didn't you tell us before?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 你怎么不早告诉我们呢?</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>int.</i></font><br>呵唷, 哎呀, 嗨<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Why, what's the harm?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 嗨, 这又有什么害处呢?</font><br>\n
wide	<h3>wide</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adj.</i></font><br>宽的, 宽阔的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He admired the city's wide streets.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他赞美该市宽阔的街道。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The gate isn't wide enough to get the car through.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这大门不够宽, 小汽车进不去。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The stream is too wide for me to jump across.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这条小河太宽了, 我跳不过去。</font><br>范围大的, 广泛的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp His interests spanned a wide range of subjects.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他的兴趣涉及广泛的学科。</font><br>完全张开的<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She stared at him with wide eyes.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她睁大眼睛注视着他。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adv.</i></font><br>充分地, 完全地<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He stood with his legs wide apart.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他两腿完全叉开地站着。</font><br>(体育中)远离目标地<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The arrow fell wide.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 箭没有射中。</font><br>\n
wife	<h3>wife</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>妻子<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Some people think that husband and wife should never work together.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 有人认为夫妻二人绝不应该在一起工作。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The two men went fishing while their wives prepared the dinner.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 那两个男人去钓鱼时, 他们的妻子做晚饭。</font><br>\n
win	<h3>win</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt. & vi.</i></font><br>(在…中)获胜, 赢, 战胜(对手)<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Which side won?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 哪一方打胜了?</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He's sure to win.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他一定会赢。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp We have won the football match.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们打赢了这场足球赛。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt.</i></font><br>获得…<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She won a bronze medal.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她得了铜牌。</font><br>(通过努力等)赢得, 博得, 获得<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp We shall win greater victories in the future.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们将取得更大的胜利。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She won her diploma in only three years.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她仅用三年时间就取得了毕业文凭。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The speaker soon won his audience.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 演讲人很快赢得了听众的好感。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp That invention won him a medal.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 那项发明为他赢得了一枚奖章。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He soon won a reputation for himself.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他很快就成名了。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>(体育比赛中)胜利, 赢<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp This season we've had three wins and two defeats.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这个赛季我们三胜二负。</font><br>\n
with	<h3>with</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>prep.</i></font><br>(表示关系)和…在一起<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Would you like to go to the street with me?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 你愿和我一起上街吗?</font><br>(表示状态)具有, 带有<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Many exhibits with characteristics of the Chinese art are on display.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 许多具有中国艺术特色的展品陈列出来。</font><br>(表示方式)用, 以, 藉<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The room is cooled with air conditioner.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这房间用空调降温。</font><br>(表示对象)对…, 关于<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She was always good with the unfortunate.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她对不幸的人总是很友好。</font><br>(表示伴随)与此同时, 随着<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I always rise with the bell.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我总是听到铃声就起床。</font><br>(表示让步)虽然, 尽管<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp With all his abilities, he failed completely.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 尽管很能干, 他还是一败涂地了。</font><br>(表示原因)由于, 因为<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She flushed with delight.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她高兴得脸上通红。</font><br>(表示态度)支持, 赞同<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Is he with us or against us?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他赞成我们还是反对我们?</font><br>(表示态度)跟(…对抗)<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp We are struggling with backwardness.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们在和落后现象做斗争。</font><br>\n
within	<h3>within</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>adj.</i></font><br>(表示位置)在…里面, 在…内部<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp There are two long rivers within the continent.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 该地区有两条长河。</font><br>(表示时间)不超过<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He has grown three inches within the last two years.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 这两年的工夫他长高了三英寸。</font><br>(表示距离)不超出<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Mr.Smith lives within ten miles of us.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 史密斯先生住在离我们不到十英里远的地方。</font><br>(表示范围)在范围[限度]内<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp It is within our power to reward him for that.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我们有权为那件事奖励他。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp There are serious differences of opinion within the medical profession.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 在医务界存在着严重的意见分歧。</font><br>\n
without	<h3>without</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>prep.</i></font><br>(表示否定)无, 没有<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I don't like a house without a bathroom.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我不喜欢没有浴室的房子。</font><br>(表示位置)在外面<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He is waiting without the door.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他在门外等。</font><br>(表示伴随)在没有…的陪伴下, 在不附带…的情况下<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The two can never talk without smiling.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他俩谈话没有不笑的时候。</font><br>\n
woman	<h3>woman</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>成年女子, 妇女<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She is a woman of great insight.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她是一个有见解的女人。</font><br>女人(女子的总称)<br>\n
word	<h3>word</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>字; 单词<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp How many letters are there in the word “struggle”?</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp struggle这个单词有多少个字母?</font><br>(说的)话, 话语, 言语<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He didn't say a word about it.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他对这件事一句话都没说。</font><br>消息; 谣言<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Word got round that he had resigned.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 谣传他已辞职。</font><br>口令, 号令; 命令<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp On his word they all moved forward.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 按照他的命令, 他们都向前进发。</font><br>诺言, 保证<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I give you my word I'll go.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我向你保证, 我会去的。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp Stand by your word.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 要守信用。</font><br>\n
work	<h3>work</h3><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>vt. & vi.</i></font><br>(使)工作<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp He's been working hard all day.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 他辛劳地工作了一天。</font><br>(使)运作, 运转<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp All the telephones don't work properly today.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 今天所有电话机都出故障了。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I know how to work the machine.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我知道如何开动机器。</font><br>(使)产生效果<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp If the scheme works, most of the peasants in this area will be rich.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 如果计划成功, 这地区的大部分农民将富起来。</font><br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The newspapers say this new drug can work wonders.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 报上说这种新药有奇效。</font><br><font color="DarkMagenta"><i>n.</i></font><br>工作, 劳动, 作业<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp I have a lot of work to do.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 我有许多工作要做。</font><br>事业<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She's devoted her life to good work.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她献身于慈善事业。</font><br>工作成果, 产品<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The villagers sell their work to tourists.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 村民们将工艺品卖给旅游者。</font><br>著作, 作品<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp She is reading a new work on acupuncture.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 她正在看一本关于针灸疗法的新书。</font><br>工厂<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp The works have closed for the Christmas holiday.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 圣诞假期, 这些工厂歇工了。</font><br>功<br><i><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp If you push hard against something and move it, you have done work.</font></i><br><font color="Navy">&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp&nbsp 如果你用力推一件东西, 并且移动它, 那你就做了功。</font><br>\n
